Japanese Army

Studies Reform of Military System 68

(Tokyo) The Army is working hard to improve the organization and equipment of its forces and to prepare emergency supplies to refresh its military appearance. It is expected to be completed by February next year. Regarding the permanentization of this, Minister of the Army Hayashi has ordered the relevant authorities to investigate, and the investigation will be conducted by the standing committee without setting up a separate investigation committee. The permanent military system is expected to be established in 1936. The disposition of the Kwantung Army is based on the opinion of Commander Hishikari, but it generally remains the same as it is now. Furthermore, the strengthening of the national air force is highly valued. A considerable amount of funds will be included in the army budget for both 1936 and 1937. Furthermore, the enrichment of air force strength and the maintenance of armaments are necessary, but the training of air force personnel and the expansion of the operating efficiency of aircraft factories are also urgent tasks and are all being addressed. (Dentsu telegram, 4th)

Conference of Local Japanese Officials: Hirota Expounds on Diplomatic Aspirations, Ostensibly Positioning Himself as Master of East Asia; Diplomacy Relies on National Support 69

(Tokyo) The third conference of local governors organized after the Saitō Cabinet's formation commenced its first day of meetings today at 10:30 AM at the Prime Minister's official residence. All ministers, including Prime Minister Saitō, were in attendance. After the Prime Minister delivered a few words, Finance Minister Takahashi and Home Minister Yamamoto delivered speeches on financial administration and local issues. The meeting adjourned at noon, and the Prime Minister hosted a banquet for the governors at his residence. The meeting resumed in the afternoon. (Chinese United Press dispatch of the 4th)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota delivered a speech at today's conference of local governors, stating in brief that modern diplomacy should not be limited to negotiations by diplomatic organs; interactions among the people are also of great importance, and he earnestly hoped that attention would be paid to this point. Secondly, Japan's assertions must strive to enhance friendship and amity with all countries. At the same time, Japan's mission in East Asia must not be forgotten even for a moment. Japan's mission is to be a force for stability in East Asia's peace. Maintaining peace and order means that East Asia should jointly shoulder this responsibility with other countries. The realization of this weighty mission is the fundamental reason for Japan's maintenance of its status as a great power. Japan sincerely hopes that China can preserve its integrity and achieve unity and prosperity, but reliance solely on external, self-centered assistance will not achieve this goal. Moreover, if a third party causes disputes in Sino-Japanese relations or takes reactionary actions to maintain peace in East Asia, Japan will by no means remain silent. Regarding recent relations between China and Japan, fortunately, China has gradually tended to understand Japan's true intentions, and it seems that relations between the two countries have now progressed to a good foundational understanding, which can be considered a satisfactory phenomenon.

The Foreign Minister then discussed trade issues before concluding as follows: In short, we will face many difficulties from now on, as it is natural for a nation and its people to encounter various difficulties when they are developing and progressing. We should be aware of this. However, the people should always act with extreme humility in all matters. In essence, diplomacy is a reflection of national strength. It is essential to expect a vigorous national spirit, unity from top to bottom, and diligent efforts to enhance national strength, as this is a fundamental condition. (Japan United Press dispatch of the 4th)

Saitō Explains Four Major National Policies: (1) The Government Intends to Actively Push Forward Various Policies, Hoping All Members Will Cooperate; First, Social Stability and Public Sentiment Must Be Ensured, and the Violent Actions of Both Left and Right Wing Factions Must Be Suppressed, Although Leftist Thought Seems to Have Been Completely Eradicated, There Are Still Potential Sources of Trouble Ahead; The Right Wing Also Uses Patriotism as a Pretext for Unruly Behavior, so Special Attention Must Be Paid to These Two Matters; (2) Local Finances Should Be Used Wisely, Administrative Systems Should Be Innovated, and the Atmosphere Should Be Refreshed; Furthermore, Education Has Recently Become Extremely Corrupt, Which Is the Cause of Unstable Thought; Fundamental Elimination Must Be Sought to Promote the Japanese Spirit; (3) Farmers Should Be Able to Live Peacefully and Make a Living, and the Central Government Should Also Conscientiously Implement Various Agricultural and Forestry Policies; (4) Under the Premise of Supporting Manchukuo, Friendly Relations Should Be Maintained with All Countries. 70

Takahashi Speaks on Financial Difficulties: Although Matters Can Be Temporarily Managed, the Emergency Situation Has Not Been Resolved; Tax Increases Can Only Be Implemented After Financial Recovery; Financial Methods Are Currently Being Investigated and Organized, and Local Finances Must Also Be Organized to Promote Mutual Advancement Between the Central Government and Localities, After Which the Balance of Financial Revenue and Expenditure Can Be Restored. (Chinese United Press dispatch of the 4th) 71

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi spoke at the conference of local governors. The following is a transcript of his instructions on foreign trade issues: Foreign trade has been quite active since the year before last. In recent years, the trade situation in various countries around the world has been extremely sluggish, but Japan's exports have made relatively active progress. This is due to rationalizing production internally and continuously exploring new sales channels externally. However, recently, various countries have adopted measures to prevent and suppress Japanese goods. If this trend continues, Japan's exports will suffer a tremendous blow. The reasoning is very clear. The laws approved and promulgated with the support of the Diet are intended to prevent the above-mentioned resistance. Regarding the formulation of the Trade Adjustment and Protection of Commerce Act, it will be used to deal with foreign countries, and the government will be granted the authority to implement appropriate measures. How to use this law will depend on various internal and external situations and must be carefully considered. (Japan United Press dispatch of the 4th)

Ariyoshi Advises Hirota to Advocate "Waterfowl Diplomacy" Towards China: Overtly Displaying Calm While Diligently Engaging in Covert Diplomacy; Simultaneously Advancing Conciliation and a Steel Blade 72

Tokyo dispatch: Ambassador to China Ariyoshi, who returned to Tokyo on the 28th of last month, visited Foreign Minister Hirota at the Foreign Ministry at 1:30 PM on the same day, engaging in talks that lasted for two hours. Ambassador Ariyoshi provided a detailed report on the progress of negotiations on pending Sino-Japanese issues and recent developments in China following the conclusion of the North China armistice agreement. In conclusion, he stated:

Outwardly Serene 73

"For diplomacy towards China, continuing to pursue 'waterfowl diplomacy' is still the wisest course, rather than moving one's feet in a flurry of activity. (Note: A waterfowl floating on the surface of the water appears calm, but in reality, its feet are extremely busy underwater. This means maintaining a detached attitude outwardly while engaging in frequent covert negotiations.) Some people advocate initiating overt and direct negotiations to resolve pending issues in one fell swoop, but this may be counterproductive." Foreign Minister Hirota listened to Ariyoshi's important advice but did not express any views.

Ariyoshi's report on the anti-Japanese movement began with the issue of boycotting goods, stating that since the North China

Incessant murmur armistice agreement, anti-Japanese sentiment and boycotts of Japanese goods in China have gradually eased. During the implementation of the "Manchukuo" imperial system, there was some resurgence. As a result of this recent informal statement to China, this movement is now likely to raise its head again. Regarding this issue, he has repeatedly requested the Nanchang government to take serious measures to suppress it whenever the opportunity for its resurgence arises. In particular, during his recent meeting with Wang Jingwei, he drew attention to the anti-Japanese speech in Beiping, the resolution of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to boycott Japanese goods, and the seizure of the Shanghai Manchukuo Yearbook, through official documents and letters.

Completing the Imperial Dream Ariyoshi further stated that during his meetings with key figures in the Nanjing government, he had repeatedly emphasized the reality of the existence of the "Manchukuo Empire." Japan's government and people have a firm belief in its cultivation and development and are providing dedicated assistance. Therefore, if China still wants to pursue the dream of the Lytton Report and change the organization of "Manchukuo," the result will only be to further complicate the situation in the Far East. Therefore, this issue should be allowed to develop naturally, separate from Sino-Japanese issues. However, the Chinese side has not yet accepted this hope, and this issue has become an obstacle to resolving pending Sino-Japanese issues.

Statement Dispute Regarding the impact of the informal statement to China on the 17th, this occurred after the meetings with Wang

Momentarily Subsided Huang and others. Before departing Shanghai, Wang sent a representative to express regret over the statement. He explained that the statement was the true intention of the Japanese Empire. Regarding this issue, it has aroused disputes in European and American public opinion, and China is probably still discussing it, but in a month or two, it will inevitably return to calm.

Nanchang Conference Regarding the content of the Nanchang Conference, there are various rumors. The Nanjing government

Various Rumors is deeply concerned that the establishment of customs offices will become a de facto recognition of "Manchukuo." The General Assembly of the League of Nations will meet on March 14, and the relationship between the Universal Postal Convention and Manchukuo will be discussed. The Nanjing government intends to use this opportunity. It seems that the Nanchang Conference did not make any specific decisions on the postal issue. (Above, by Gaironsha)

Report on Progress promulgated last summer, the Japanese side has

Continued to protest the "Tariff Issue." The amended tariff rate has a trial period of one year and will inevitably be amended again when it expires. "Sino-Japanese Liaison Issue" The Sino-Japanese liaison issue has been pending since 1929. China has firmly opposed this proposal, citing that "it has not concluded such treaties with other countries," and it is currently difficult to realize. "Trade Issue" After the Manchurian Incident, the import of Japanese goods into Guangdong Province was absolutely prohibited. Recently, it has been possible to import them openly, but due to the bankruptcy of rural villages, it is difficult to expect an increase in trade with China. "Organization of Old Loans" According to recent investigations, due to the financial difficulties of the Nanjing government and the exhaustion of the financial world, it is impossible to quickly organize the claims of the Empire and its subjects against China. Therefore, there is currently no good method other than to take a wait-and-see attitude.

Page 8

France to Propose Dissolution of the Disarmament Conference; The League of Nations is Feared to Be Dragged Down; Britain Plans to Strengthen its Military 75

(London) Secret intelligence from Paris states that France will propose the dissolution of the Disarmament Conference when the General Disarmament Commission reopens in Geneva on May 29. It has been learned today that the British government has received this news. In the past week, the British Cabinet's Special Disarmament Committee held three secret meetings, and its intentions are now revealed. Those close to government circles declare that if the Disarmament Conference fails, the British Cabinet will definitely consider a plan to strengthen British military power, especially the Air Force. Responsible parties declare that the government has now decided to adopt a guarantee of implementation of the disarmament convention, but this is conditional on France and other related countries taking concrete steps towards disarmament. Observers say that the British government's efforts to mediate the Franco-German deadlock are now exhausted, so if France indeed puts the Disarmament Conference to death, the British government has no choice but to increase its national defense capabilities. International diplomatic circles are very worried about this news, believing that the day the Disarmament Conference fails will be the day the League of Nations collapses. (National Telegram of the 4th)

British Cabinet Subcommittee Discusses Disarmament Issue; If a Convention Cannot Be Reached, the Only Option Is to Form an Alliance with France 76

(London) The Cabinet's Subcommittee on Disarmament Issues met this morning. In light of Germany's rearmament, which has become a reality, British public opinion hopes that a disarmament convention can be signed, even if the scope of the convention is limited to Western Europe. However, public opinion is aware that France cannot be satisfied with empty promises, so it also supports the determination of methods to guarantee the implementation of the convention in Geneva. Conservative newspapers recently stated that Britain only has two paths to follow in the disarmament issue: (1) Sign a disarmament convention; (3) Form a defensive alliance with France. In general, people originally did not particularly support the second option, but today, views have changed, and they all believe that if a disarmament convention cannot be established, the only solution lies in forming an alliance with France. (Havas dispatch of the 3rd)

(London) The Cabinet's Subcommittee on Disarmament Issues reconvened this morning at the Prime Minister's Office on Downing Street, chaired by Prime Minister MacDonald. (Havas dispatch of the 4th)

Eden Answers Questions from Parliamentarians

Britain Has No Intention of Abandoning Naval Agreements 77

(London) The House of Commons met this afternoon. Conservative Party member Marsden raised the question of whether the British government would "declare the Washington Naval Treaty void before December 31 of this year in accordance with Article 23 of the treaty." Keeper of the Privy Seal Eden replied, "The government currently has no intention of declaring the Washington Naval Treaty void." Recently, British conservatives have been vigorously advocating that Britain should break free from the constraints of various treaties so that its naval development is not restricted. Yesterday, Lord Lloyd, the former High Commissioner to Egypt, said so at a meeting of the British Navy League. (Havas dispatch of the 2nd)

Summoning an Imperial Defense Conference: The Government Avoids Giving a Clear Answer 78

(London) British conservatives are advocating that an Imperial Conference be convened in the short term to discuss Imperial economic and defense policies. This advocacy is now gaining momentum. Today, a Conservative Party member in the House of Commons asked Prime Minister MacDonald whether he had considered the suggestion of Bruce, the Australian Commonwealth's representative in Britain, to convene an Imperial Conference next year to discuss economic and defense policies. MacDonald avoided mentioning this matter, saying only that he was unaware of such a suggestion and that "the date of the Imperial Conference should be jointly decided by the governments of the relevant territories." Some members of the Conservative Party expressed dissatisfaction with the Prime Minister's response. (Havas dispatch of the 3rd)

Germany Rearming its Air Force: Seeking to Create an Air Hegemony in Europe; British and American Industries Supply Materials - American Newspaper Reveals News - 79

(New York) The "Nation Weekly," which has a liberal tendency, recently published an article revealing the fact that British and American industries are assisting Germany in rearming its air force. It stated that several American factories are dedicated to assisting Germany in building the largest air fleet in Europe. The factory has sent three representatives, all of American nationality, who are currently stationed in Berlin to negotiate everything. Furthermore, the Hitler government has ordered necessary parts from British and American companies to manufacture 2,500 new-style bombers and fighter planes, some of which have already been delivered. This fact is known to diplomatic circles stationed in Berlin, and it is also heard that Germany is currently working overtime to build airplanes. Several American factories often receive urgent telegrams from Germany requesting prompt delivery. The newspaper also stated that at the aviation exhibition currently being held on Unter den Linden in Berlin, banners are posted that read "Germany's future lies in the air," and express Germany's hope to quickly achieve this goal. (Havas dispatch of the 4th)

Australia Strengthening its Defense: Allocating Funds to Order Airplanes from Britain; and Will Hold Naval Maneuvers; The Scheduled Plan of the Singapore Conference Completed 80

⊙Melbourne The Australian Commonwealth Minister for Defense, Mr. Parkhill, announced today that the Australian government has allocated £345,000 to order airplanes from a British airplane company. This matter is being carried out in accordance with the recent decision of the Australian Cabinet, which advocates strengthening coastal and naval defenses and will hold naval maneuvers. It is heard that this new plan is the result of the Singapore Conference held several months ago. (National News Agency dispatch of the 4th)

Trade War Between Britain, America and Japan: Britain Will Terminate the Anglo-Japanese Trade Treaty in West Africa; America Studies Changing its Trade Policy; Japan Also Decides on its Response Measures 81

(London) British businessman Sir Simon and Japanese Ambassador to Britain Matsudaira met today to discuss the competition between Japanese goods and British goods in British colonies. Thus, efforts to seek Anglo-Japanese understanding have taken another step forward. Although official circles are keeping silent about this meeting, Reuters has learned that Sir Simon told the Japanese ambassador that Japanese goods are sold at extraordinarily low prices, so the British government will find ways to protect the British textile industry and other industries from further invasion by Japanese goods. This plan will inevitably proceed unless Japan immediately changes its attitude. The protective actions deemed necessary by the British government are unavoidable and are hoped to provide a path to resolving the Anglo-Japanese cotton industry deadlock soon. The British government has been slow to adopt protective actions in its own country and colonies for more than a year, solely to create the best possible atmosphere for Anglo-Japanese commercial talks. Now, if Britain actually takes protective actions, it is only because commercial agreements seem to have no hope of being established, or because textile talks show no signs of revival. Londoners believe that Japanese exporters enjoy a temporal advantage, so the British government's protective measures must not be indefinitely delayed, but must be limited to a period of time to prevent British commerce from suffering severe damage when talks resume in the future. It is heard that the British businessman informed the Japanese ambassador of several proposals that require a response from the Japanese government. Some say that the meeting between the British businessman and the Japanese ambassador has revealed the breakdown of Anglo-Japanese commercial discussions, but official circles today do not take this view. It is also heard that the British government will notify the Japanese government on May 16 that the trade treaty between Japan and the British colonies in West Africa will be terminated one year from now. (Reuters dispatch of the 3rd)

(Tokyo) Regarding the memorandum of British businessman Sir Simon of England regarding Anglo-Japanese commercial consultations, it was telegraphed to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs by Ambassador Matsudaira in England this afternoon. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately held a leadership meeting to discuss what opinions should be expressed. The content of the memorandum has not been made public, and it seems to be quite unfriendly. The Japanese government believes that if the export distribution of British cotton cloth is not done automatically, the British government will cooperate with its colonies to implement orders restricting the import of Japanese cotton cloth. Therefore, the Japanese foreign affairs authorities are quite dissatisfied. As for when Japan's response will be issued, it has not yet been determined. It will probably criticize the unfriendly attitude of the British government and urge the British government to promptly propose concrete proposals for a friendly solution. (Dentsu dispatch of the 4th)

(Washington) Japanese goods are flooding the South American market, and American exporters are therefore very concerned. They now hope that President Roosevelt will use the pending tariff bill to conduct reciprocal trade negotiations to assist American exporters in competing with Japanese goods. On the one hand, the United States wants to maintain most-favored-nation treatment, and on the other hand, it wants to negotiate reciprocal tariffs with foreign countries, which has aroused a strange feeling among diplomats from various South American countries here, because they do not know how this contradictory thing can be accomplished. After studying the United States' foreign commercial policy, the Pan American Union believes that tariff negotiations to increase special commercial relations between the two countries seem to be inconsistent with the most-favored-nation principle at first glance. The Roosevelt government now believes that conducting tariff negotiations with foreign countries under the most-favored-nation clause has the possibility of restoring international commerce, and at the same time can maintain the United States' policy of treating all foreign countries equally in commerce for the past eleven years. The committee appointed by President Roosevelt to draft the United States' permanent commercial policy recently reported, acknowledging the need to adjust the national economy to suit world trends. The report also classifies American industries based on the effectiveness of the entire country and the relationship of foreign trade. This change in American commercial policy has made South American diplomats express optimism, believing that there is a possibility of reciprocal trade between the United States and South America. (National Telegram of the 3rd)

(Washington) Officials from the State Department and the Department of Commerce heard the news of Britain's opinions on Japanese competition and did not find it strange, but they believed that unless the competition became more intense, the general economic situation in the world, the anti-dumping laws, and the gentlemen's agreement prohibiting unfair competition between the United States and Japan would not make it necessary for the United States to take any severe commercial war actions against Japan. The agreement reached a few days ago to reduce the import of Japanese pencils is one example of the methods used by the United States to avoid commercial wars. According to this agreement, Japan restricts its exports of pencils to the United States to 125,000 gross (144 pieces per gross) per year, a decrease of 35,000 gross compared to last year. Similar agreements on other Japanese goods are currently under negotiation. (Reuters dispatch of the 4th)

American Tax Bill

Delivered to Roosevelt for Signature: Tax Increases for the Rich, Tax Cuts for the Poor 82

(Washington) The tax bill, which has been debated for more than two months, was completed today and sent to President Roosevelt for signature. The Senate today also rejected the Quinn amendment to increase income tax by 10 percent. The tax bill passed today increases taxes on the rich, and there are no changes for ordinary people, or even reductions. The bill will have an impact on the import of coconut oil from the Fiji Islands. Congress expressed satisfaction with reducing taxes for ordinary people and increasing taxes for those who live on securities dividends. Senator La Follette's amendment proposed increasing inheritance tax on the rich, but estates under US$40,000 are tax-free, and estates over US$40,000 are taxed on a progressive basis from 1 percent, up to 60 percent for estates over US$10 million. This item alone can increase government revenue by $85 million. The bill also stipulates that income tax is 4 percent. The bill also imposes heavy taxes on the gains of private companies and large sums. Another amendment to the bill authorizes the President to increase the tax on the branches of foreign companies in the United States by 50 percent for foreign countries that discriminate against American people and American commercial firms. According to the proposer, this is aimed at France. The current capital gains and losses law also stipulates that all assets that have not changed for more than one year must be taxed, and when these assets are sold, regardless of profit or loss, 80 percent must be taxed. (National Telegram of the 3rd)

Former US Treasury Secretary

Woodin Passes Away from Illness 83

(New York) Former Treasury Secretary Woodin passed away last night due to nephritis and uremia, followed by throat disease that was unresponsive to medical treatment, at the age of 66. Woodin was originally a great industrialist with a large accumulated wealth. After President Roosevelt took office in 1933, he served as Treasury Secretary. He encountered a banking crisis at the time and relied heavily on his rescue efforts. Later, he resigned and retired due to disagreements with President Roosevelt. (Havas dispatch of the 4th)

(New York) Mr. Woodin, the former Treasury Secretary under President Roosevelt, has passed away today after suffering from a throat disease for a long time since he resigned from his position due to illness. Throughout his life, he devoted himself to business. In his prime, he worked for a railway materials company and a bank. Before Roosevelt became president, he assisted him in various matters and provided much help. Later, he was also one of the President's brain trusts. He served as Secretary of the Treasury. He was known for his musical expertise and was a famous American composer. He liked to collect books and antiques and also enjoyed fishing, sharing the same hobby as Roosevelt. He was born on May 27, 1868. He originally belonged to the Republican Party and later joined the Democratic Party. His estate is estimated to be between US$2 million and US$20 million. (National Telegram of the 3rd)

Hitler Centralizes All German Police Power: A New Ministry is Established with Göring as Head 84

(Berlin) It was heard today that the cabinet is currently considering establishing a new German Police Ministry, with General Göring as Minister and the newly appointed Secret Police Chief Himmler as his secretary. This is another step by the National Socialist Party to centralize all German police power. Himmler has already gained control of the political police and secret police in all German states. Although General Göring has resigned from his position as Minister of the Interior of Prussia, the police power of that state is still in his hands, as this power has already been transferred to the Premier of Prussia. (Reuters dispatch of the 3rd)

Demise of the Japanese Fascist Faction: Ichiki Appointed President of the Privy Council; Hiranuma's Power Suffers a Major Blow 85

(Tokyo) As a result of discussions between Prime Minister Saitō, Elder Saionji, Grand Chamberlain Yuasa, and Minister of the Imperial Household Makino, Baron Ichiki Kitokurō was recommended as President of the Privy Council yesterday. The important intention is to restrain the power of Vice President Hiranuma's faction, and at the same time to expect to sweep away the forces of the anti-constitutional and pro-military faction. However, Vice President Hiranuma had already been secretly plotting to overthrow former President Kuratomi and expected to be promoted to President in accordance with the tradition by the Vice President (i.e., Hiranuma himself), but Elder Saionji broke the precedent and recommended Ichiki, arguing that the new President Ichiki had once served as Vice President. Therefore, in order to organize the ranks of the constitutional faction, Hiranuma Vice President and his faction will be removed. However, Hiranuma has expressed extreme dissatisfaction and may resign automatically. The military and Hiranuma's faction have close relations. How the conflict between the constitutional faction and the military faction, centered on the Privy Council, will end is worthy of attention both at home and abroad. (Chinese United Press dispatch of the 4th)

(Tokyo) Ichiki Kitokurō's appointment as President of the Privy Council is a break from tradition, as the President of the Privy Council has always been promoted by the Vice President. However, Ichiki served as Vice President during the era of President Hamao, so it can be said to be a natural order. After President Kuratomi's resignation this time, the Hiranuma Vice President faction, which had been expanding its power within the Privy Council, will inevitably decline. In the future, the atmosphere within the Privy Council will attract attention from all sides. According to some observations, Vice President Hiranuma is extremely dissatisfied with Ichiki's appointment as President, so it is possible that he will resign at an appropriate time in the future. (Japan United Press dispatch of the 4th)

Muslim country warring with each other

Han Zhi Defeats Yemen, Advances Straight Along the Red Sea Coast, Nearly All of Arabia Falls Under Control, Rumors of the Yemenese King Being Assassinated Unconfirmed, Three British Warships Arrive to Protect Nationals 86

(London) The Kingdom of Hejaz in Arabia is at war with Yemen. Yemen has suffered a defeat and abandoned the town of Hodeidah. There are 300 British nationals in that location, mostly Indians. There is a risk that their lives may be harmed by the Arabs. The British government is paying close attention. It is reported that the British warship 'Bonsons' has arrived there to provide protection. Also, the British cruiser 'Indus Enterprise' set sail for Aden this morning, presumably in connection with the war between Hejaz and Yemen. After the Yemeni troops were defeated by the Hejaz troops, the tribal people of the Arabian desert gathered in the mountains around Hodeidah, fearing that the town would be ravaged by these people after the Yemeni troops withdrew and before the Hejaz troops arrived. As a warning, British military aircraft circled the town in the sky several times today. London officials claim that who wins or loses is irrelevant to Britain. What is feared is that the war may endanger the lives and property of British nationals. Although Kamaran Island near Hodeidah is not a British territory, the quarantine station there is related to Britain, as this station is jointly operated by the British and Dutch governments to check for epidemics among those coming from the Dutch East Indies to Mecca. At the same time, according to news from Cairo, the Imam of Yemen, in order to avoid Muslims killing each other, has withdrawn his troops stationed in the disputed area and has requested the King of Egypt to step in as a fellow believer to mediate and restore peace. (Reuters telegram, 3rd)

Aden - The troops of King Ibn Saud of Hejaz are advancing victoriously along the Red Sea coast. Now, apart from a few small principalities, almost all of Arabia is under his control. Ibn Saud has long cherished the dream of unifying Arabia, and the time for realizing it seems not far off. The troops of the Imam of Yemen, known for their elite status, have been unable to recover after being defeated by the Hejaz army. It seems that their territory will soon be incorporated into the territory of the Hejaz. Three British warships are currently docked in the Yemeni port of Hodeidah, and all foreign nationals there have been moved to Kamaran Island. The rumor that the Imam of Yemen was assassinated by rebellious subordinates has not yet been officially confirmed. However, it is reported that the Imam fainted due to depression while convening a meeting. When the troops under his command heard the news, they lost their will to fight, and suffered a disastrous defeat. (Reuter's telegram from this agency, 4th)

Cairo - The rumor that the King of Yemen has been assassinated has been found to be untrue today. The King of Yemen has sent a telegram to the King of Egypt requesting the start of peace talks. (National News Agency telegram, 4th)

Under Japanese Puppet Oppression

Farmers' Economy Bankrupt, Exorbitant Taxes Emerge Endlessly, Income Cannot Cover Expenses 100

Harbin Correspondence: Northeast agricultural soybean production originally ranked first in the world. The prosperity of the Northeast also came from soybeans. However, since Japan created puppet organizations, righteous armies have arisen, and there have been endless military disturbances. Exorbitant taxes have emerged endlessly. In addition, agricultural freight rates are extremely high, and farmers are really overwhelmed. Now, due to the overproduction of soybeans, soybean prices have fallen miserably. Each "fudu" (equivalent to 30 kg) is only worth about two or three jiao. After deducting shipping and transportation costs, farmers receive almost nothing. As a result, the countryside is on the verge of bankruptcy. Here are the facts obtained from the investigation:

Water Transportation Costs 101

The transportation costs from the center of Harbin, per

fudu, are all calculated in current silver dollars.

The value and transportation costs of soybeans are listed below:

Location Soybean Price Shipping Cost

Fujin 3 jiao 1 fen 2 jiao 4 fen

Jiamusi 3 jiao 5 fen 2 jiao

Yilan 3 jiao 9 fen 1 jiao 8 fen

Railway Transportation Costs 102

Regarding the facts of railway transportation costs:

There are 750 cars of soybeans held up in Suihua. The market price per fudu is 4 jiao, and the transportation cost to Harbin is 1 jiao 2 fen. There are 100 cars in Hailun. The market price is 3 jiao, and the transportation cost is 2 jiao. There are 1,200 cars in Taian Town. The market price is 3 jiao 1 fen 5 li, and the railway transportation cost to Dalian is 6 jiao 1 fen. There are 400 cars in Keshan. The market price is 2 jiao 2 fen, and the transportation cost to Lianbu is 6 jiao 4 fen. Since the transportation cost is already like this, the soybean price is eroded by the transportation cost, and almost nothing is left. One can glimpse the plight of the farmers.

Exorbitant Taxes 103

The various taxes paid by farmers include:

National tax 5 jiao, security maintenance fee

3 fen 7 li, mountain forest guerrilla fee 1 jiao 3 fen, Heilongjiang province tax 1 fen 2 li, totaling 6 jiao 7 fen 9 li. In addition, Baojia fee 6 jiao, police fee 2 jiao 6 fen 7 li, education fee 3 jiao 7 fen 1 li, totaling 1 yuan 2 jiao 3 fen 6 li. The above totals 1 yuan 9 jiao 1 fen 5 li. This is the situation in Heilongjiang. The other provinces are similar.

Farmers' Income and Expenses 104

Farmers' income and expenses per "xiang" (equivalent to 10 mu):

Labor wages 12 yuan, cattle and horse farming fees 10 yuan, miscellaneous expenses 2 yuan, totaling 24 yuan. On the income side, assuming that each xiang can harvest four shi, and each shi is 3 yuan, then the income per xiang is only 12 yuan. In addition, if you deduct the horse-drawn cart transportation cost to the station, then each horse-drawn cart, assuming it carries a large shi, and calculate the incidental miscellaneous expenses, each cart can reach 3 yuan, then what is left? It is no less than farming and losing money. If it is for sale, there are many expenses. Also, every 100 yuan of sales proceeds must pay a police fee of 2% and an education fee of 1%, totaling 3%. In addition, it is necessary to deduct farmers' living expenses, entertainment expenses, and self-defense expenses, etc. The degree of loss is self-evident. The plight of farmers in the Northeast can be imagined.

Southern Route Army Eliminates

Remnant Bandits South of Junmen. Frontline Troops Deploy Defense Works, All Agencies Donate Funds for Local Relief. 105

Guangzhou Correspondent: I have just received a telegram from the front: On the 24th, Huang Shitu's regiment recaptured the bandit strongholds of Wushi and Xiashizai, capturing more than ten bandit officers and soldiers and more than seventy guns. There were more than a hundred scattered bandits on the mountain of Dihui Rock. After being surrounded and suppressed by Ye Gang's regiment, they retreated to Huichang on the night of the 21st. Dozens of bandits were left to guard the mountains. On the morning of the 24th, it has already been completely resolved. On the 21st, Xie Zheng's regiment's first and second battalions were sent to occupy the bandit strongholds of Dasanggang and Lazhudi one after another, killing more than two hundred bandits. Lian Dangsheng's regiment captured the bandit stronghold of Huangshadong River on the 21st. Now, the bandits in the area south of Junmen Ridge have been completely eliminated. It is said that the Communist bandits have gathered their remnants since being severely damaged in Junmen, and have requisitioned small groups from various places, totaling more than 30,000 people, led by the bandit leader Zhu De. They are concentrated in Ruijin, Yudu, and Huichang, and plan to counterattack in three routes. In addition to ordering the frontline troops to deploy defenses, the Second Column is stepping up the construction of fortifications to contain the westward invasion of the Yudu Communist bandits. Miao Peinan, Chief of Staff of the Southern Route Army Headquarters, went to Meixian the other day to meet with Li Yangjing, Commander of the Second Column, to discuss the overall plan for suppressing the bandits. The entire plan has been agreed upon and reported to Chen Jitang. Li Yangjing then set off from Meixian at 10:00 am on the 25th to inspect defenses around Junmen. After Li Yangjing arrived at the front line, he reported yesterday that the main force of the Red bandits guarding Junmen had been defeated and fled, and is now gathered in Huangkengdong in Ruijin, where they have established a fake headquarters. The Communist bandits suffered heavy casualties in Junmen this time, with only more than 2,000 people left. The baggage and equipment have been almost completely lost.

Both ammunition and food are scarce. The miscellaneous grains in the former bandit area have been looted. It is reported here that the front line has been ordered to step up the deployment of defenses and handle the aftermath. The Seventh and Eighth Divisions have made great contributions to the recapture of Junmen and have been given a reward of 10,000 yuan from the Headquarters to reward the officers and soldiers who contributed to the two divisions. Also, because the Junmen area has suffered from the Communist bandits, the people are suffering. The political training offices of the Seventh and Eighth Divisions are ordered to rush to handle the aftermath and organize the Baojia system. The Provincial Government also resolved on the 27th to donate some money from the savings of various agencies to relieve the displaced people in the bandit area near Junmen Ridge. It was immediately decided that the Guangdong Provincial Government would donate 1,000 yuan, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau 1,000 yuan, the Provincial Bank 1,000 yuan, the Guangdong-Hankou Railway Bureau 1,000 yuan, the Agriculture and Forestry Bureau 500 yuan, the Tumin Earth Factory 1,000 yuan, the High Court 300 yuan, and the Anti-Smuggling Headquarters 500 yuan. The money will be remitted to the Commander-in-Chief's Office and handed over to the front for handling. (April 28)

He Chengjun Goes to Northern Hubei Again to Inspect, Convenes a Meeting of Generals to Deploy Military Affairs Against Bandits, The Border Blockade Measures Have Been Approved and Implemented by Chiang 107

Hankou Telegraph: He Chengjun, the Pacification Commissioner stationed in Hubei, previously received a telegram order from Chairman Chiang to go to Xiangfan to deploy defenses against Sichuan bandits and to supervise the suppression of the remnant bandits led by Ma Xiyou, Wang You, and Liu Guitang. He also convened Xu Yuanquan, Zhang Ming, Zhang Zhenhan, Fan Shixing, and others, giving them instructions and assigning them to suppress the bandits separately. Before long, Bandit Liu fled to Henan, and Wang and Ma also suffered heavy losses. The construction of the blockhouse highway project to defend against Sichuan bandits has also been accelerated. He then received a summons from Chiang to go to Jiangxi to report on the inspection and deployment situation. Chiang said that northern Hubei borders several provinces and has a strategic location, so he instructed He to go there to oversee and control all parties. Recently, Wang and Ma's remnant bandits have returned to northern Hubei and have shown signs of resurgence. Therefore, He went north again at 10:00 am on the 2nd. He arrived in Yuan'an in the afternoon of the same day, inspected Xiao Zhichu's troops, and decided to go to Pinglin Temple, on the border between Anlu and Yingcheng, on the 3rd to inspect Rong Jinfang's troops. Then he will follow the Hua Road to Fancheng. In addition to continuing to inspect the blockhouse highway and set a deadline for completion, he will also convene a military conference in Fancheng with generals such as Xu Yuanquan, Fan Shisheng, Zhang Zhenhan, Rong Jingfang, and Luo Qijiang to discuss ways to thoroughly eliminate bandits.

He Chengjun had previously submitted five proposed implementation measures for the border blockade in Hubei Province to Chiang: (1) According to Article 1 of the Proclamation, the designated blockade areas in the Hubei border area, belonging to Zhuxi, Zhushan, Fangxian, and Badong counties, are all adjacent to bandit areas. (2) In accordance with the blockade measures for neighboring bandit areas, blockade management offices should first be established in the county towns of Zhuxi, Zhushan, Fangxian, and Badong counties, and management branch offices should be established in Quanxi in Zhuxi, Baihe Lu and Liushudian in Zhushan, Jiudaoliang in Fangxian, and Dafengyi in Badong. The county governments should investigate the situation and set up inspection cards and build blockhouses at other important passes to Sichuan. Each inspection line should be divided into various routes connecting bandit areas. (3) In addition to setting up blockade management agencies, each county should set up a food, salt, and kerosene public sales committee in its respective areas. The county governments should determine the number of sub-committees based on local conditions and submit them for approval. Regarding salt, Zhuxi, Zhushan, Fangxian, and Badong have always been supplied by imports from Sichuan. The county governments should pay special attention to this and prevent it from being transferred to bandit areas. (4) The establishment of blockade agencies should be organized jointly by local military and political leaders and local gentry, and should be handled in accordance with the blockade regulations issued by the Nanchang Camp. (5) The head of each county should supervise the handling of the blockade situation each month and report it to this office on schedule so that it can be reported to the Headquarters of the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui for reference. Subsequently, Chairman Chiang gave the following comments: "The proposed implementation method for the Hubei border area blockade is generally feasible. However, Item 3 mentions the establishment of food public sales committees in each county town. The public sale of grain should be postponed unless absolutely necessary. You should comply with this." Now, the Pacification Headquarters has ordered all localities to begin implementation. (May 2)

Songjiang 108

Mother-in-Law and Daughter-in-Law Force Daughter-in-Law to Hang Herself

Xu Fugeng, a resident of Xiang 30, Chenjiahang Township, only had one daughter, named Suying. Last year, she married A-Cai, the eldest son of Zhang Zhong, a resident of the same township. At the beginning of the marriage, their relationship was harmonious, but the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law had eccentric personalities and often abused Suying. When she returned home to complain to her father, he always advised her to go back and live with him. On the 15th of the lunar month, Suying died suddenly. It was reported to Xu Fugeng, who went to see the body and saw rope marks on the neck, which seemed like murder. So yesterday he came to Songjiang to request the prosecutor's office to investigate. Prosecutor Meng accepted the complaint and led officials to the countryside for inspection, and summoned relevant witnesses. According to the report, she was forced to hang herself to death. It was ordered that the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law be released on bail pending investigation.

Grains and Cakes Industry Association Appeals to the Provincial Government 111

The Fengjing Town Grains and Cakes Industry Association, due to the increase in business tax on wholesale sales, has repeatedly telegraphed the Finance Department to maintain the order. Now, dissatisfied with the Finance Department's approval, it has filed an appeal to the Provincial Government. The facts and reasons for the appeal are excerpted as follows: "(1) Facts: It has been found that members of the association, Zhang Chengtai, Dinghua Company, Peng Hengyi, and other three companies, are operating in Fengjing Town, engaged in the wholesale of bran, not retail sales. The business tax of these three firms has always been paid at half the rate according to regulations, that is, one per thousand. On March 2nd of this year, the Songhu Jin Business Tax Bureau forwarded an order from the Finance Department stating that the bran industry, regardless of retail or wholesale, should uniformly be taxed at two per thousand. After the association listed the reasons, it successively telegraphed the Finance Department on Jiang Hanri's behalf, requesting that the original plan of collecting taxes according to regulations be maintained. The approval received stated that Jiang Hanri's telegrams were fully understood (omitted below), and that the request did not comply with the regulations and was difficult to approve. The above is the situation of this case. (2) Reasons: The change of bran business tax to two per thousand was implemented in the winter of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Before the implementation until December of the 22nd year, the bran wholesale business was still taxed at half the rate, one per thousand, which is in line with the provisions of Article 11 of the newly revised business tax regulations. Now that this article has not been changed, the Finance Department only increased the tax from one per thousand to two per thousand from this spring onward, intending to increase the tax on bran wholesale to two per thousand, which inevitably regards Article 11 of the new regulations as a mere formality. It should be known that the change of the grains and cakes tax to two per thousand was out of the government's consideration for people's livelihood. According to the law, it is a matter of grace. Wholesale and retail are matters of law and order. The relationship between law and order and the government's prestige cannot be affected by the granting of grace. This is very clear. Even as the original approval said, then Article 11 of the new regulations should be deleted or changed, otherwise, what does the original text mean by 'those who have retail business and also wholesale shall not use this as an excuse to pay half tax'? What does 'trickery' refer to? Based on the above reasons, in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of the Petition Law, an appeal is filed, and in accordance with Article 11 of the same law, it is requested that the execution of collecting two per thousand be immediately stopped, and that half the tax be collected in accordance with Article 11 of the new business tax regulations, to comply with the law."

Jiading Branch Director Suspected of Releasing Criminals and Arrested 116

After Guan Xiuzhao, the former director of the Nanxiang Public Security First Branch, left office, Li Yiru, the former director of the Department of Civil Affairs, was directly appointed by Gu Renfa to take over. Li appointed Zhao Jinda, the son of Zhao Fujiang, a well-known rogue in the town, as the detective. Most of the detectives were also apprentices of Zhao Fu, and they continued to collude with each other. Zhao had three sons who set up gambling dens in places such as the teahouse in the main hall of the Great Temple and the Pacific Hotel, engaging in various illegal activities. Xue Bingyang, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, learned of this and specially dispatched Inspector Bao Jingyu on the night of the 2nd, leading 18 inspectors, officers, detectives, and police officers to the town at 11:30 PM. More than 20 gamblers, including Zhao Fujiang and Li Yunggu, and three opium smokers were captured in the Pacific Hotel, along with opium and gambling paraphernalia. The next day, more than 10 suspects, including Wang Xiaoliu, a large package of red pill ash, eight large jars of opium ash, a large box of playing cards, three sets of mahjong tiles, a cash box (with separate compartments for different denominations), two sets of pai gow tiles, a list of gambling hosts, and more than 20 pieces of accounts and ledgers for selling opium were seized in Zhao's residence. There was also a book of unauthorized levies collected in the town, named the Huoyin Company, which stated that the monthly income was 200 yuan. The people and the loot were all taken to the town's branch bureau, and it was already dawn. However, Zhao Fujiang, the main suspect who had been detained at the bureau, had escaped again. Director Li of the branch bureau said that he was being watched by Patrolman Ma when he escaped. The bureau director Li Yiru, Patrolman Ma, and Li Yunggu, Wang Xiaoliu, and 13 others, along with the loot, were taken to the bureau to prepare a document and send it to the county. Magistrate Xu believed that Li Yiru had allowed his subordinates to sell opium and gamble, and now he was suspected of harboring the main suspect. He immediately ordered the detention and investigation. Patrolman Ma and Li Yunggu and the other five people were also detained on suspicion of serious crimes. The others were interrogated and released on bail. County Magistrate Xu awarded 5 yuan each to injured police officers Cao Dengming and Wang Yulin for their courageous service.

Wuxi: Spring Silkworms Begin First Sleep Early 117

Due to the impact of the sluggish silk market, the prospects for this year's spring silkworm cocoons are not optimistic. Therefore, fewer farmers are raising them than last year, resulting in a significant decrease in the sales of silkworm eggs. This year, various farms in Jiangsu Province produced a total of over 700,000 sheets of silkworm eggs, with Zhejiang being the strongest in selling them. In this area, about 100,000 sheets have been sold, and there are still over 100,000 sheets in stock, mostly miscellaneous brands. Merchants are extremely anxious about the hatching status and are selling them off cheaply at 1.6 yuan per sheet, which is unprecedented. The old brands, such as Tiger Brand and Longevity Star Brand, are only selling for 7 jiao per sheet. In the past two days, the early helping has collected flowers, and the local varieties in Dongting, Zha Jiaqiao, Qianzhou Bei Qifang, Yuqi Fuzhou Village, and other places have all begun their first sleep. Improved varieties will also be collecting flowers soon. Mulberry leaves in the four townships have no market price yet.

Reorganizing Provincial Roads 118

The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, because Chairman Jiang's Southeast Transportation Tour is approaching, should reorganize the highways that have already been completed in the province. Those that have not been completed should be supervised by the Highway Administration to rush construction. Famous scenic spots, historic sites, and municipal facilities in various counties should also be reorganized. The roadbed and earthwork project of the Xihu Road Xiyu section undertaken by the local Construction Bureau started on the 25th of last month. Since the start of construction, the project has been progressing smoothly, and about 20% has been completed. It is expected that the entire section will be completed by May 15th. The other two roads, Xi-Cheng and Xi-Yi, have already been completed and are open to automobile traffic. However, they also need to be maintained to be perfect. The Wuxi section of the Xi-Yi Road, from the intersection of the Xi-Cheng Road to Huishan, has not yet been paved. It is currently being organized by the Jiangnan Long-Distance Bus Company, which is paving a gravel road surface. About 40% of the materials have been prepared, but there are difficulties in transportation. Once everything is ready, construction will begin immediately. It is planned to use Sanhe soil for grouting and then pave gravel. Recently, the company has purchased 20 diesel oil tarpaulin vehicles from Shanghai to expand its business, which are expected to be transported around the 2nd of this month.

Homicide Case to be Solved Within a Time Limit 120

Yu Mourong, a butcher from Caijiachang near Fubridge in Wuyi County, was robbed of over a thousand yuan by bandits and shot eight or nine times, resulting in his death. It is learned that after the incident, the local area was greatly shocked. The body has been inspected by the county prosecutor, and relatives of the deceased were interrogated on the 3rd. Public security authorities went to investigate and conduct a detailed study. It is believed that this case is merely a case of robbery by bandits and actually contains elements of revenge killing. Skilled detectives have been dispatched to strictly arrest the murderers for interrogation. Sun Fukang, the director of the responsible Public Security First Branch, requested a severe punishment for his negligence in prevention. The county government has approved the recording of a major demerit and ordered the case to be solved within seven days. At the same time, the county bureau has issued announcements and offered rewards for the arrest of the murderers, offering 300 yuan for each person captured.

Jiangyin Orders Expedited Land Investigation and Reporting 121

The county government previously received an order from the Finance Department to conduct land investigation and reporting. With the active efforts of County Magistrate Bao, the project has actually been completed. However, due to a request for correction submitted by the Yixing Association of Fellow Townsmen in Beijing to the Ministry of Finance, and the telegraphic order from the Cheng County Party Department and various public groups to the county to handle it carefully, the Ministry of Finance instructed the Finance Department to investigate and respond. Now, a response has been submitted, and County Magistrate Bao was telegraphed, stating that someone has submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to postpone the land investigation and reporting. The reasons why it is inconvenient to postpone have been reported to the Ministry. You should continue to supervise your subordinates to expedite the work and complete it on schedule, without delay. However, punishment for exceeding the deadline may easily arouse public resentment and should be handled by the county at its discretion. After receiving the telegram, County Magistrate Bao has forwarded it to the district chiefs for compliance.

Nantong: Temporary Martial Law Imposed Along the Coast to Suppress Bandits 122

There are maritime bandits causing trouble in various coastal areas of Jiangbei. The province has ordered the maritime guerrilla team to suppress them. Team leader Shen Fengshan has led his team out to sea from Yancheng to the waters around Lvjue to suppress them severely. In order to prevent bandits from infiltrating, temporary martial law has been imposed in each area.

Responsibility Issues for Official Escape 123

Hu Jinlong, a police officer who harbored opium traffickers, was being interrogated judicially and held in custody at the Public Security Bureau. However, after the court sentenced Hu to life imprisonment, news suddenly broke that he had escaped. The local community was outraged. The chief prosecutor of the court, Liu Shizhu, will request the Public Security Bureau to hand over the person as soon as Hu's execution period arrives. The County Party Department has sent a special letter to the court and the county government stating that this case cannot be concluded ambiguously, and special attention should be paid to the issue of responsibility.

Zhenjiang: Pilgrims Robbed by Thugs 124

Lin Zhongzhe, a 32-year-old from Fujian, once served in the military in Fujian Province. He came to Zhenjiang to visit friends and stayed at the Shunxing Inn near the Danyang Wharf in Ximen. Lin was a devout Buddhist. On the morning of the 2nd of this month, he went to the Wanfu Palace in Changshan, ten miles south of the county, to offer incense and worship Buddha. On his way back to the city after the event, more than a dozen thugs suddenly appeared on the way through Banshan, blocking the road. They robbed Lin of the dozens of yuan he was carrying, as well as a central party card, a pen, a sanitary sweater, a leather suitcase, and a felt hat. The thugs stabbed him with a knife on his leg and forehead, causing him to fall to the ground and unable to walk. Fortunately, pilgrims at the scene saw this and carried him back to the city for treatment. They also reported the incident to the military and police authorities in charge, requesting the arrest of the thugs and bringing them to justice.

Headless Male Corpse Found Outside the North Suburb 125

A headless male corpse was found in Wangjiawan, outside the North Gate of this city. Nearby residents reported it to the Zhenjiang Local Court, which dispatched prosecutor Zhu Daiguang, along with a clerk, coroner, and police officers, to inspect the scene. The corpse was lying on the ground. It was very tall, about thirty years old, and headless. The upper body was naked, and the lower body was only wearing a pair of dirty pants stained with blood. The ground was covered in blood, and the situation was extremely terrifying. It seemed that he had been murdered and the body abandoned there. No relatives have claimed the body so far. The village chief has been ordered to prepare a coffin and collect the body, and the military and police authorities have been asked to investigate the murderer in this case.

County Magistrate Sentenced to Imprisonment for Malfeasance 126

Jiang Fuyuan, the former magistrate of Funing County, was sued in the Provincial Department by Qiu Fuchu and other citizens of the county in the spring of the previous year for illegally detaining good citizens and embezzlement. The Provincial Department removed Hong from office and placed him under surveillance for more than a year. Subsequently, the Provincial Government was reorganized, and a large number of officials under surveillance in the province were transferred to the court for interrogation according to law. It is reported that after several investigations by the local prosecutor's office of the court, an indictment was filed based on Hong's confession. On the 25th of last month, the debate was declared over. Because the evidence of Hong's crime was conclusive, Hong Fuyuan was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment and fined 1,000 yuan.

Yangzhou: Three Houses Burned Down in Fuxi Street 127

Zhao Er, a man from Haizhou who worked as a pushcart operator, accidentally caused a fire at his home on Fuxi Street in the old city of Yangzhou at around 11:00 AM on the 3rd due to carelessness in cooking lunch. The fire spread to the homes of Lu Kaiyuan from Huaicheng and Zhou Er, who lived together. In a flash, the flames soared into the sky and everything was turned to ashes. Fortunately, they were all thatched houses, and the fire was quickly extinguished by the water dragon, without affecting the nearby tile houses. However, they were still greatly alarmed.

Haimen: Major Fire at the Third Factory Market 128

There were more than 30 thatched houses in the West Market of the Dasheng Third Factory, which were the residences of workers. Yesterday (the 2nd), at around 4:00 PM, Huang Yinlang, a worker, caused a fire while cooking dinner. The fire quickly spread, alarming the entire city. The security guard of the industrial company and the fire brigade rushed to the scene to put out the fire. However, due to the dry weather and strong winds, it was not easy to contain the fire, and all the thatched houses were turned into ashes.

Ningbo: Worker on the Ningheng Road Kills Villager 129

Xu Afu, a villager from Dasong Township in Yin County, made a living by rowing a boat. On the afternoon of the previous day (30th), at around 1:00 PM, he was transporting a boatload of rice from Dasong to Jinji Bridge to unload. After arriving at the destination, Afu's rice boat accidentally collided with the pier, leading to a dispute with workers building the Ningheng Road. The dispute escalated into violence. Afu was outnumbered and was struck in the head several times with stones by the road workers, causing him to fall into the river. He was rescued by his brother-in-law, Zhang Xingcai, but due to the severity of his injuries, he died at midnight. The perpetrators, Zhu Xiaogou and the other three, have been turned over to the Yin County Local Court for interrogation.

Reconstruction of Old Jiang Bridge Begins 130

The reconstruction of the Old Jiang Bridge project began with an opening ceremony at around 9:00 AM on the previous day (1st). Yu Qiaqing and County Magistrate Chen held the groundbreaking ceremony. Committee members from the Shanghai and Ningbo preparatory offices and the general manager engineer of Siemens Company were also present. After the ceremony, they went to the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce for a luncheon and held a joint meeting of the Shanghai and Ningbo preparatory offices. Wang Wenhan was re-elected as the director of the preparatory office. It was also agreed that the losses beyond the original price of the houses and land to be demolished on both sides of the bridge would be treated as donations and included in the memorial. The engineers are currently measuring the area of both sides of the bridge, and construction will begin as soon as the measurements are completed.

Cihe Road to Open to Traffic on the 10th 131

The Cicheng to Hetoushi Highway has been completed. The Lixing Company, organized by merchants and civilians, has contracted to handle traffic matters. The Cixi County Government has notified the towns and villages along the line that it will open on the 10th of this month.

Special Report

On the Issue of Promulgating the Constitution - A Reply to Mr. Wu Jingxiong - Zhang Yuanruo 132

In my previous article, "A Fair Discussion on the Constitution Draft," which appeared in the newspapers in Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, I received overflowing praise from Mr. Wu Desheng, the Vice Chairman of the Constitution Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan, especially regarding the conclusion on the promulgation of the Constitution, which greatly humbled me. Due to pressing matters, I have not yet responded. Now, the period for public comment on the Constitution Draft is about to end. Looking at the comments from all parties, most are biased towards criticizing the articles, words, and sentences. Those who can conduct sincere and practical discussions on the promulgation and implementation of the Constitution, which is more important, are very few. I am deeply afraid that this constitutional project will repeat the failures of previous constitutionalism. With concerns in my heart, I cannot help but speak out. Therefore, I have written this article again to offer my humble opinions. For years, my argument has been based on governance (see my book "On Law"), but law is not constitution-making, and even less should it be repeated constitution-making. Chinese constitutionalism has a history of several decades, and repeated constitution-making has occurred more than once. The splendid constitution has almost gathered the best of the world, but its achievements have only seen the destruction of law and order, resistance and destruction. Not only has it failed to achieve the effect of faithful adherence and long-term stability, but it has also left a bad impression of "fickleness" and "changing one's mind" in the public's psychology. Therefore, the previous constitutions were only strategies for the authorities to clean up the situation and decorations to embellish the facade. The people also had no connection between the constitution-making and their own rights and happiness (see the preface to my book "Modern Constitutionalism"). This is the fundamental reason for the failure of constitutionalism in our country over the years, and it is also the historical lesson that today's constitution-making authorities should seriously learn from.

Frankly speaking, there is no need to rush into constitution-making at this time. In terms of the "use" of the constitution, the constitution is a historical product and cannot be arbitrarily created and implemented. In terms of the "form" of the constitution, our country already has a constitution, such as the Outline of National Reconstruction, the Organic Law of the National Government, the Provisional Constitution for the Period of Political Tutelage of the Republic of China, and the Outline of Political Tutelage. If the whole country has the spirit and determination to abide by and believe in the law, then our country has already reached the realm of constitutionalism. Furthermore, the model countries of modern constitutionalism, such as Britain and France, have fragmentary and sporadic constitutions, published gradually. The British constitution is a collection of the Magna Carta of 1215, the Petition of Right of 1628, the Habeas Corpus Act of 1679, the Bill of Rights of 1688, the Act of Settlement of 1700, the Parliament Act of 1911, the Representation of the People Act of 1918, and the amendment of 1928. The French constitution is only a collection of the Organic Law of the Senate of February 24, 1875 (Articles 1 to 7 of this law have been repealed by the law of December 9, 1884), the Organic Law of Public Powers of February 25, the Law on the Regulation of Public Powers of July 16, the Law on the Election of Senators of August 2, the Law on the Election of Deputies of November 30, the Law on the Capital of Paris of July 22, 1879, the amendment to the Law on the Election of Senators and Deputies of December 9, 1884, the amendment to the Law on Elections of June 16, 1885, the Law on Incompatibility of Members of Parliament of December 26, 1887, the Law on Candidates of July 17, 1889, the Law on Military Obligations of Members of Parliament of July 2, 1895, the Law on Preventing Electoral Fraud of 1902, and the various articles of April 2, 1903, February 17, 1908, March 23, 1914, March 31, January 5, 1918, October 17, 1919, August 10, 1926, July 10, 1927, July 21, December 30, 1928. Therefore, the constitution does not need form, but only "faith" and "observance." The legalists said that "bad law is better than no law," which is a deep understanding of the essence of the rule of law.

Then, shall we dissolve the Constitution Drafting Committee and destroy today's existing Constitution Draft? This is also not possible, and this kind of unrealistic argument should not be accepted by those who can fairly discuss politics. Speaking of the matter as it stands, now that there is a Constitution Draft, we must only seek to avoid repeating the past mistakes and be able to implement it effectively. Therefore, I believe that the focus of today's constitutional issue is not on how perfect the articles of the constitution should be, but only on how the promulgation and implementation should be regulated so that a win-win situation can be achieved. The provisions of the Founding Father regarding the promulgation of the constitution in the Outline of National Reconstruction are very solemn. One is: "The draft constitution should be based on the Outline of National Reconstruction and the achievements of the two periods of political tutelage and constitutional government. It should be discussed and revised by the Legislative Yuan and publicized to the people at any time for selection and implementation when the time comes" (Article 22 of the Outline). The other is: "When more than half of the provinces in the country have reached the constitutional period, that is, when the local autonomy of the entire province is fully established, a national assembly shall be convened to decide on the constitution and promulgate it" (Article 23 of the Outline). Therefore, the greatest prerequisite for the promulgation of the constitution is the completion of local autonomy. The completion of local autonomy requires: "A clear census of the population of the entire county, a complete survey of the land of the entire county, proper handling of police affairs in the entire county, successful construction of roads across the four borders, and its people have been trained in the use of the four powers and have completed their national obligations, and those who swear to carry out the revolutionary doctrine may elect county officials to carry out the political affairs of the county and elect representatives to discuss and establish the laws of the county, to become a completely autonomous county" (Article 8 of the Outline). Secondly, "the people shall have the right to directly elect officials, the right to directly recall officials, the right to directly initiate laws, and the right to directly reject laws" (Article 9 of the Outline). Furthermore, the organ that decides on the constitution is the National Assembly, and the election of the representatives of the National Assembly must wait until "after the establishment of local autonomous governments in each county" (Article 14 of the Outline). The convocation of the National Assembly must also wait until "more than half of the provinces in the country have reached the constitutional period" (Article 23 of the Outline). Our country has not yet completed the political tutelage and has no achievements in local autonomy. It is naturally dangerous to prematurely promulgate the constitution at this time. It must be known that the Founding Father's division of the national reconstruction program has its own rich experience, far-sighted vision, and profound knowledge. The realization of constitutionalism cannot be achieved merely through empty words, nor can it be expected overnight. It must be ensured that civil rights are fully developed before there can be a solid and unshakeable constitutional foundation for thousands of years (see pages 86-87 of my book "Overview of Modern Politics"). This principle of national construction is not only suitable for our country's national conditions, but also can be used as a reference for constitutional reform in various countries around the world. We must not underestimate ourselves and rush ahead, disrupting the steps of national construction (to be continued).

Vice President of the Judicial Yuan

Tan Zhen to Sail Abroad Today 137

Focusing on the Abolition of Consular Jurisdiction, He Will Go to Turkey for Investigation. Judicial Yuan President Tan Zhen has been ordered to go to Europe and the United States to investigate judicial matters. He first went to his ancestral home in Taoyuan, Hunan Province, and then came to Shanghai with his wife and daughter. He has now purchased tickets for the French postal ship D'Artagnan, and together with his entourage of eight people, including his secretary, will board the ship in Shanghai at 2 p.m. today to sail abroad. Our reporter visited President Tan last night to inquire about his views on the overseas investigation. President Tan was then engaged in calligraphy, and Secretary-General Yang Boshen was entrusted to relay everything. The main points are recorded as follows:

Departing Today 138

Mr. Yang said that when Vice President Tan served under President Sun Yat-sen as the Provisional President during the early years of the Republic, he was ordered to go to Europe to investigate judicial matters, but it did not materialize. Therefore, this subsequent order to go abroad can be said to be fulfilling his long-held aspiration. All overseas passports, etc., were handled directly by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which was relatively convenient. All ship tickets, etc., have also been fully prepared. It is scheduled to embark at the French Company Wharf on the Bund of the French Concession at 2 p.m. today, take a small steamboat to board the D'Artagnan and sail abroad.

Accompanying Personnel 139

Accompanying Vice President Tan to Europe and the United States are English Secretary Yang Boshen, French Secretary Li Jing'an, German Secretary Jian Zan, and Secretary Song Zhenlü, a total of four people. Song Zhenlü is the eldest son of Mr. Song Yufu. He was originally employed at the Audit Yuan and was transferred by Tan to serve as an attendant this time. In addition, Tan's wife and daughter, and his son-in-law Wu Xianshu, also travel on the same ship, but only as far as Hong Kong, and will then take the land route.

Recent Photo of Tan Zhen (Provided by the Far East Agency)

One-Year Term 140

Vice President Tan's investigation in Europe and the United States this time is scheduled for one year. The established investigation itinerary is to take the D'Artagnan to Marseille, then remain in France for inspection, then to Italy, Spain, Switzerland, Germany, Austria, then to Turkey, then from Turkey to Soviet Russia, then to the Netherlands, Belgium, then to Northern Europe and the United Kingdom, across the Atlantic to the United States, then through South America: Argentina, Brazil, Peru, Chile, and then return home.

Scope of Investigation 141

According to Mr. Yang, representing Vice President Tan's views, the focus of this investigation is on the judicial administration, court organization, and prison conditions of various countries, for reference in our country. Special attention will be paid to the current civil and criminal laws of various countries and their characteristics. The constitution is the fundamental law of the country, and special importance will also be attached to the constitutions of various countries. During the investigation, he also wishes to exchange opinions with jurists from various countries to assist in the improvement of the judiciary.

Longer Stay in Turkey 142

Next, he said that our country is constrained by unequal treaties, mostly due to the inability to abolish consular jurisdiction. The impact of this extends to the inability to recover inland navigation rights, the inability to fully control tariffs, etc., leading to the country's weakness. Therefore, this investigation places greater emphasis on abolishing consular jurisdiction. In the future, after arriving in Turkey, the period of investigation will be longer than in other countries. Because Turkey is a newly emerging country that also suffered from the pain of consular jurisdiction in the past, the experience of its years of struggle, and the current judicial improvements, are greatly instructive for our country. Therefore, a longer stay in Turkey is planned.

Calligraphy on a Screen 143

According to Secretary Yang, our visit to various countries will involve a longer stay in Europe than in the Americas, because world jurisprudence, such as Roman law and Continental law, is concentrated in the European continent. The reporter also inquired whether he would go to Japan for investigation upon returning home. Mr. Yang said that he might not go at that time. Yesterday, Vice President Tan wrote a congratulatory screen at his residence for his niece's wedding. The words were "The peach tree is young and tender, its blossoms radiant. This maiden marries, may she bring harmony to her home." Sixteen characters, followed by "I am ordered to go to Europe this time, and will send my friend's niece, Youlian, to Guangdong on the way, to marry Junfu. Written to celebrate," the strokes are very majestic.

Guo Chuntao, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Industry, has been ordered to go to Europe and the United States to investigate industries. All preparations have been completed. Mr. Guo took the overnight express train from Beijing to Shanghai the day before yesterday, arriving at 7:30 a.m. yesterday morning. He went to his hotel to rest and decided to take the French postal ship D'Artagnan this afternoon to sail abroad, first to Marseille, then to various countries to conduct investigations. Departing Today to Investigate Industry and Commerce 145

Mr. Guo first said that the Ministry of Industry, in view of the current decline of industry and commerce in our country, urgently needs to find ways to remedy the situation. Therefore, I am specially dispatched to various countries to investigate the state of industry and commerce, to serve as a reference for future remedies. It has now been decided to depart on the French postal ship D'Artagnan tomorrow (the 5th) for an investigation period of more than half a year. Paper Factory Solely Run by the Government. The Newsprint Factory planned in Wenzhou is also actively underway.
