Refutation of the Breach of the Fenglou Dike 152

The Office of the Engineering and Relief Group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee of the National Government sent a telegram to the New Voice Society from Kaifeng yesterday morning, stating that they had read a report in the Kaifeng Henan Republic Daily and the Northern Daily, citing a dispatch from Tianjin on the 2nd, stating that Fenglou had breached again. After investigation, the Fenglou stone dam was closed and connected, and the Stone Village main dike was also blocked and connected. A water-blocking and air-tightening dam was also built at the Yaotou location behind the stone dam, which was also completed last month. All are now stable and there has been no breach. Please quickly disclose this so that those who care about river affairs may understand the truth. The east and west dams have been connected into one, and the flow outside the dike has been cut off for many days. In addition to restoring the original height of the dike, more than 20 li of the dike bank from Shitou Village to Dacheji has been approved by the group to be raised and thickened. Construction is currently underway to raise it more than two meters above the flood level of 1933.

The International Trade Bureau Announces Last Year's

International Trade and Domestic Economy 157

International Economy: Chaotic in the First Half, Hopeful for Recovery in the Second Half 158

Domestic Economy: Extremely Weak, Rural Areas Increasingly Bankrupt 159

The Shanghai branch of the Shenshi News Agency reports that the International Trade Bureau has compiled and statistically analyzed the status of China's international trade for the entire year of 1933 and has prepared a detailed report for submission to the Ministry of Industry. The report is excerpted as follows:

Submission to the Ministry of Industry: The International Trade Bureau's Report on the Actual Conditions of International Trade in 1933 states: 160

"Respectfully submitted, the total import value for the whole year of 1933 was 134.5 million yuan, a decrease of 16% compared to the previous year. The total export value was 61.1 million yuan, a decrease of 20% compared to the previous year. The import surplus was 73.3 million yuan, a decrease of 18% compared to the previous year. However, this year, there were no statistical reports for the entire year from the Northeast customs. In 1932, the first half of the year still included figures from the Northeast customs. As the scopes are different, it is difficult to compare. If the Northeast figures for the first half of 1932 are removed and compared with this year, imports decreased by about 11% compared to the previous year, while exports increased by 6%. The reason for the decrease in imports is not due to the increase in domestic consumption of Chinese goods, which replaced foreign goods, but rather due to the bankruptcy of the domestic economy and the weak purchasing power of the people in recent years. In addition, the implementation of the new Japanese tariff on May 22 of this year also had a considerable impact. In terms of exports, excluding the Northeast, although exports slightly increased, the amount was small and there was no stable trend. It is difficult to predict whether it can continue to be maintained in the future. As for the nature of commodities, imports this year were still mostly manufactured goods. Due to the lack of figures from the Northeast customs, the disastrous drop in soybean exports caused significant changes in exports. Currently, manufactured goods account for 44.9% of exports, ranking first. However, this phenomenon is merely a change in the composition of the numbers and is not sufficient to indicate the trend of China's export trade. The situation of industrial products is no different from that of previous years. The nature of China's foreign trade still maintains the trade pattern of an industrially backward country that has existed for decades. Its backwardness deserves attention. We hereby compile a report on the trade conditions for the third and fourth quarters and the entire year of 1933 for your review. Respectfully submitted, Chen, Minister of Industry, He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, May 1934."

International Economic Report 161

Regarding the International Economic Overview of 1933, 1933 was the Fifth Year of the World Economic Panic. 162

In this year, due to the efforts of various countries to seek relief, the economic situation, although still chaotic in the first half of the year, showed signs of recovery in the second half of the year. From a national perspective, the situation in the United Kingdom was the best. Since President Roosevelt implemented an inflationary monetary policy in the United States, the national economy has suddenly become active. However, it is difficult to say whether this artificial result can be maintained for a long time. Due to currency contraction in France, although production has slightly increased, prices have continued to fall. Germany has also made progress in recent years. Japan, due to the benefits of exchange rate depreciation, has seen continued rapid progress in production and trade. The Soviet Union began its second five-year plan this year and has laid a solid foundation for the coming year.

Overview of the Domestic Economy 163

Regarding the overview of the domestic economy in 1933, although the economic situation in various countries in the world has shown signs of recovery this year, China's economic situation has deteriorated further than before. In the past few years, the world's economy has declined, prices have fallen, industry and commerce have been depressed, and trade has declined. China's price level, due to the impact of falling international commodity prices, could have declined along with it. However, because China is a silver-using country, the rate of decline in the price of silver exceeded the general price decline in gold standard countries. China's purchasing power was further reduced by the price of silver, and the national situation showed no signs of improvement. Not only was the Northeast not recovered, but there was almost no moment of stability even within the borders. At the beginning of the year, there was the loss of Yuguan, the fall of Rehe, and the unrest in Beiping and Tianjin, followed by the Chahar incident, the Yellow River flood, and the Fujian coup at the beginning of winter, leaving the people with no opportunity to rest and recuperate. The rural economy became increasingly bankrupt, the people's purchasing power became increasingly weak, and commodity prices continued to decline.

Trade Report Published 164

The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has been publishing a trade report every six months since 1932, detailing the domestic and foreign economic overview and China's foreign trade situation. Since its publication, it has been highly praised by society. The trade report for the third and fourth quarters of 1933 has now been published. The entire book consists of more than 120 pages, approximately 80,000 words, divided into two parts. The first part records the international economic overview and the domestic economic overview. The second part details the import and export trade figures, the trade of import and export commodities by country, and the trade of import and export commodities by port, and includes 58 types of statistical tables and 6 statistical diagrams. It is an important reference book for those who are concerned about China's foreign trade. In addition to submitting the report to the Ministry of Industry and distributing it to various agencies, there are not many copies left. The previous trade reports published by the bureau led to numerous requests from people from all walks of life, and later requests could not be fulfilled. In order to impose a slight restriction, each copy is now charged 5 jiao in silver. Those who are concerned about China's international trade should purchase it as soon as possible to avoid missing out.

Feng Bingnan and Others Act as Mediators 177

The Xinzhapu Police Station of the Public Concession, fearing a conflict, dispatched a large number of detectives to suppress it. In the morning, tenants in the neighborhood asked the church for water, but the priest refused to connect the hose, which led to a dispute. Fortunately, no trouble was caused. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, they went to the water company with Feng Bingnan and others to negotiate the restoration of the water supply. Regarding the water fee, it is guaranteed by the tenants in cash. The company has not yet fully accepted it and is still under negotiation.

Method for Changing Inspection of Medicines: To Benefit Travelers and Alleviate Merchants' Difficulties, Shanghai Municipal 185

The Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the New Medicine Association stating that according to a letter from member Zhongfa Pharmacy, it was learned that the police stationed at the North Station are detaining travelers carrying Western medicines, regardless of whether they are prohibited or not, and transferring them to the court. After the medicines have been sent to the Municipal Health Bureau for testing, a verdict will be made. When the association first heard about this, it was very surprised. Just yesterday, a retail customer purchased two pounds of salicylic acid and took a train to Xi. He was also caught in this trouble. Later, the customer managed to notify the association.

After sending staff to explain to the district, they were released on bail. It was claimed that during the detention, there were many other detained people, and a large number of goods from various Chinese, Western, and international brands were confiscated. It seems that many people have been affected. Under such circumstances, customers from other cities will not dare to come to Shanghai to purchase goods, and the impact on our industry will be significant. Even the police officers in the district feel that this method is troublesome and advocate that our industry association should forward a letter to the municipal chamber of commerce, which will then send a letter to the municipal government, ordering the health bureau to appoint special personnel to be stationed at the station to assist in the inspection, so that they can be identified. This will not only avoid increasing the suffering of legitimate merchants and travelers,

and it will also be possible to effectively combat the transportation of prohibited drugs. This relief method is indeed urgent, so the association is writing based on the facts and requesting that the municipal chamber of commerce immediately forward a letter to the municipal government, urging it to change the inspection policy, or order the health bureau to send personnel to inspect with the police, so that they can be distinguished on the spot, in order to benefit travelers and alleviate merchants' difficulties, etc. The association has found that the inspection of medicines must be carried out by someone who recognizes poisonous drugs in order to make a detailed identification. If medicines are seized as soon as they are seen, regardless of whether they are prohibited or not, and all of them must be tested to determine whether they are prohibited, then merchants and civilians will suffer endlessly. Therefore, the association is writing to your association to forward it to the municipal government, urgently ordering the health bureau to add personnel who are familiar with medicines to be stationed at the station for inspection, so as to avoid disturbances, etc.

Trial Opens in the Case of Pirated Books from Kaiming Bookstore 193

Two books published by Kaiming Bookstore, "Grammar and Composition," were discovered to be pirated. The person who confessed to the piracy, Yang Jingye, was arrested by the Huishan Police Station, and 1,000 copies of the pirated books were seized at the Datong Binding Factory on Dalianwan Road. The police station filed a public prosecution. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, a retrial was held in the third court of the first division of the Shanghai Special District Local Court. First, the police station's lawyer stated that the printer of the book, Wang Lansheng, the owner of Hongxing Printing Factory, had been summoned. According to the defendant Yang Jingye's confession at the police station, the original book was first submitted to the printing factory for printing, and then the cover and copyright page were also submitted to the factory for printing separately. Although Wang Lansheng did not know which company published the book when printing the original book, the cover and copyright page clearly had the Kaiming Bookstore trademark and the words "Published by Kaiming Bookstore." Therefore, Wang Lansheng is actually an accomplice. However, the book's binder, Chen Zhaozhi, and the cover printer, Yin Chunrong, are also related to this case. They were not summoned and should be rescheduled for another hearing. Judge Zhan then asked the defendant Yang Jingye about his confession, which was consistent with the police station lawyer's statement. He also asked the second defendant, Wang Lansheng, who claimed that the book was submitted to him for printing by Chen Weisheng (Zhaohuan) of Wenshu Bureau. The book was only called "National Language." After it was printed, the book was taken out of the Datong Binding Factory, and the paper plates were sent to Wenguang Bookstore. However, the cover and copyright page were not printed by the factory, etc. Later, the plaintiff Kaiming Bookstore's representative lawyer, Cha Renwei, claimed that the book's paper plates were important evidence in the case. Also, Chen Weisheng of Wenguang Bookstore is an important criminal in the case and should be arrested and investigated. The court announced that the retrial would be held next Friday.

Domestic Electrical Appliances Are Not Inferior to Imported Goods 196

Domestic electrical appliances have made rapid progress in recent years, which has led to price cuts and oppression from foreign competitors. In April last year, foreign electrical light bulbs were heavily discounted. However, the Yabuer brand light bulbs, made in China, did not drop in price due to the support of the Chinese people. This year, foreign light bulbs have made a third drastic price cut. Yabuer brand light bulbs still maintain the same price without any reduction. Shanghai Red Pill Poisonous Atmosphere Spreads

Seven dens raided in one day, red pill poisoning is spreading throughout Shanghai, hoping that the police authorities will do their utmost to eradicate, three cases in the southern city 198

Yesterday morning at around 1:00 AM,

the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective

Team Leader Lu Ying received a tip that three places in the second district, near the South Railway

Station, including No. 34 Derun Lane, No. 7 Huairen Lane on Meixie Road in the southern city, and No. 80 Huixiang Lane on Liyuan Rear Road, were secretly manufacturing red pills and providing lamps for people to smoke, requesting that officers be dispatched immediately to arrest them. Upon hearing the report, Team Leader Lu immediately ordered Shen Wenda, the leader of the second district, to lead several police officers from the second district to arrest them at the specified addresses. A total of two people were arrested at Derun Lane, including Ren Teng, a young woman from Ningbo, and Wang Ruisheng from Zhenjiang. A large amount of evidence, including red pills, guns, and lamps, was seized. Only three small packets of red pills and one gun and lamp each were found in the pavilion room at No. 7 Huairen Lane on Meixie Road. Red pill criminal Yin Laosan escaped. When they arrived at No. 80 Liyuan Road, only Wu Shimu, a native of Jinhua, was arrested. He confessed that there was a secret manufacturing den in the next door at No. 82. They immediately went to arrest them and seized a vice, baking cage, and wooden plates used for making pills, 28 packets of red

pills, totaling 14,000 pills, more than 13 catties of loose pills, and 19 catties of raw materials. The criminals Gu Jingen, Xu Fuming, Mrs. Xu Zhang, and Mrs. Wu Wang were arrested and taken to the district together. The criminals then confessed that their accomplice Sun Jingen was in the French Concession. The officers then worked with detectives from the French Concession police station to arrest Sun at his address. After questioning them one by one, they were sent to the Third Division for review along with the evidence and the criminals in the afternoon.

One case in Zhabei 199

The Detective Team of the Zhabei Fourth District Public Security Bureau, yesterday at

12:20 PM, received a tip that someone was running a den for selling drugs such as red pills and opium at No. 24 Fuan Lane, Xinmin Road, requesting that officers be dispatched immediately to arrest them. The female criminal claimed to be Guo Zhang, 35 years old, and lived with Guo Qingxiang. Both admitted that the red pills were purchased from the concession and admitted to providing them for smoking, but denied selling them. After reviewing the confession, the interrogator ordered them to be sent to the Zhabei branch of the Third Division of the Public Security Bureau along with the opium pipes and red pills, and then transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for interrogation.

After the Court Session on Debt Disputes

Gao Xiaochen Punches Tao Jiayao, Tao Suffers Internal Injuries and Vomits Blood, Court Reopens for Trial After Recess - Gao is Ordered to be Released on Bail for Assault in Court - 204

Tao Jiayao, a Jiangxi native residing at No. 1877, Avenue Joffre, French Concession, previously filed a private prosecution against Gao Xiaochen in the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court for fraud. After several summonses by the court, the details were reported in previous newspapers. This case was continued for trial again in the afternoon of yesterday. Both parties arrived with their lawyers. Originally presided over by Judge Tu Shenjie, the case was transferred to Judge Xiong Huiping of the same level, so a renewed trial was declared. After questioning both parties about their age, origin, and occupation, Gao Xiaochen, the plaintiff, stated the reasons for the prosecution. The judge asked Tao, "You and the plaintiff are friends of many years, why must you litigate? Can both parties make concessions and reconcile to avoid litigation fatigue?" Tao replied, "I am nearly seventy years old and have been sued for criminal fraud for no reason. I am unwilling to accept this. I have already filed a counterclaim for false accusation. If you consider friendship, Jiayao is willing to guarantee the plaintiff's loan of one thousand yuan from Hengli Bank, which I will repay on his behalf." Then, the lawyers of both parties debated for a long time. The court ordered both parties to retire and try to reconcile outside, pending a rescheduled hearing. Thereupon, both parties complied and retired, and the judge also announced the adjournment. However, as Tao Jiayao stepped out of the courtroom and was walking halfway down the stairs, Gao Xiaochen, the plaintiff, suddenly became angry and rushed up, punching Tao's back violently. Fortunately, two bailiffs, No. 529 and No. 93, saw it and stepped forward to stop him, preventing Tao from falling. Gao also stopped. After Tao went downstairs and retreated into the lawyer's lounge, he vomited blood due to internal injuries.

At that time, Tao's lawyers, Luo Jiaheng, Wang Zaoshi, and Li Guozhen, witnessed the situation and immediately reported to Judge Xiong, who then reopened the second court and summoned Gao Xiaochen to the case, reprimanding Gao for being so unreasonable and committing assault in the court. He was ordered to be released on bail, pending Tao Jiayao filing another lawsuit. It is reported that Tao's injuries are quite serious, and he is now at home seeking medical treatment. At the same time, he has asked Lawyer Luo et al. to draft a petition and submit it to the court, requesting an injury examination, and filing a private prosecution against Gao Xiaochen for assault.

Someone in the Court Actually

Throws Feces at a Lawyer, Fortunately, a Briefcase Provided a Shield - This Actually Happened in Court 205

A lawyer from a certain law firm at No. 368 Jiangxi Road, whose business is usually quite prosperous, inevitably made enemies. Yesterday morning, the lawyer was entrusted by Sheng Yu, the former manager of the Qian Sanxin Yarn Factory, to go to the First Special District District Court to defend Sheng in a case where he was accused by the factory's workers. At 11:45, the case was being heard in the Eleventh Court. The lawyer, dressed in legal robes and carrying a briefcase, went straight to the Eleventh Court from the lawyer's lounge. Unexpectedly, he was surrounded by eight plaintiff workers accusing Sheng Yu as he approached the entrance to the court, their momentum fierce. Seeing this, the lawyer, fearing that these people might take some drastic action, explained in advance that he was only representing Sheng on duty and did not ask about other issues. If there were any expressions, they should be directed to Sheng. Unexpectedly, at this moment, two people in the crowd suddenly held huge packages wrapped in yellow paper and threw them at the lawyer's face. The lawyer had been prepared, so he immediately raised the briefcase he was carrying to shield his head and face. As the paper packages collided, the paper package immediately broke, and the contents were all filth, splashing on the lawyer's head, face, and body. The thrower, still unsatisfied, continued to try to force the remaining package into the lawyer's mouth. Fortunately, the briefcase provided a shield, not tasting the fragrance. Seeing that the goal had been achieved, the thrower left calmly. At that time, because the lawyer did not make a sound, no one paid attention. It was not until the perpetrator had gone far away that the lawyer reported to the court authorities and requested an investigation. It is unexpected that in a place of judicial dignity and strict security, such an illegal madman would commit such an outrageous act, which is truly shocking.

Cheng Rongde, 47 years old from Sijing, has been setting up a fish stall in the Nine Acres Vegetable Market. He has a son named Ada, who is now 17 years old. Unexpectedly, Ada punched his father again. Rongde grabbed a sharp blade and stabbed Ada under his left armpit, about several inches deep. Ada was in extreme pain and fell into a pool of blood. Rongde intended to kill his son, so he did not allow rescue. When Li Zhi, the nineteenth watchman of the area, arrived, he took the injured Cheng Ada to Renji Hospital for treatment. It is said that the injury is quite serious and may be fatal. However, Rongde went out after killing his son. When Rongde returned at 7 pm, the police arrested him and took him to the office for questioning. After questioning by Director Shen, the case involved killing a son and causing injury, and he was ordered to be handed over to the General Bureau for handling according to the law.

Jiang Ali

Suspicious Gunshot Wound - Voluntarily Seeking Treatment at the Hospital - The Reason Remains Unclear 208

At about 7:30 pm yesterday, the Fifth District Third Sub-Office of Zhabei suddenly received a call from the Avenue Haig Public Concession police station, stating that Jiang Ali, a Gaoyou native, 32 years old, had voluntarily sought treatment at Tongren Hospital for a gunshot wound at about 7 pm, claiming that he had been ambushed at the intersection of Avenue Haig and Yangjia Creek Road. When asked about his address and occupation, he was vague. Therefore, the hospital detained him and reported to the police station, saying that the place was under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District Third Sub-Office, so they were notified, hoping to thoroughly investigate. After receiving the news, the sub-office immediately sent police detectives to investigate the Yangjia Creek Road area and asked the shops to inquire whether they had heard or witnessed any shooting cases. The shops all said that there had been no changes. The detectives went to various roads to check for bloodstains on the ground, but were disappointed. At the same time, no bullets or shells were found. Therefore, they suspected and immediately returned to the office to report. At the same time, the director of the sub-office went to the police station with the detectives to Tongren Hospital to question Jiang in detail about the cause of the injury. He claimed that he had come to Shanghai from Gaoyou with his wife the day before yesterday and was currently living at the house of his friend Xie Meichang at No. 6 Tianyi Lane, Tiantong Road, Zhabei. This afternoon, when passing through the intersection of Avenue Haig and Yangjia Creek Road, he was shot and hit in the abdomen. He had no occupation. When asked about other things, he was vague. The director of the sub-office immediately returned to the sub-office and sent police to Tianyi Lane to ask his friend Xie Meichang. He learned that Jiang Ali had returned home on foot after being injured. His wife discovered that he was injured and asked him to seek medical treatment. How he was injured, he didn't know at all. Therefore, this case was still a mess when the reporter drafted the manuscript. The suspicious point is that Jiang Ali claimed to have come to Shanghai the day before yesterday and was very poor. Why did he have four pawn tickets from pawnshops on Avenue Haig in the French Concession and other places, totaling more than thirty yuan, and the earliest one was pawned on March 15th? At the same time, why was there no trace of bullet shells or gunshots? Therefore, others speculated that Jiang Ali's injury may have been caused by infighting among accomplices.

Rail Bureau Tours

Revised Convenient Method for Round-Trip Tickets - and Able to Get Off Midway 210

For the convenience of passengers, the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration will, from May 10th, issue joint tour round-trip tickets for the two lines, as well as tour round-trip tickets for each station on this line. Whether it is the outbound or return trip, it can be used on any day within the validity period. The valid return date is calculated from the date of departure of the train, not the date of arrival. For example, a revolving guest holds a Shanghai North Station to Nanjing round-trip ticket sold on May 1st. The return portion is valid for the train to Shanghai from Nanjing on the night of the 7th at 12 o'clock. Although the ticket has expired when it arrives in Shanghai, it is still not considered expired because the train departs within the seventh day of validity. Also, the return portion does not need to be re-stamped with the date and train number at the station. When passengers purchase this round-trip ticket, if they declare that they need to stop midway, the station selling the round-trip ticket can also handle it separately.

Chicken and Duck Industry

Foreign Code Account Dispute Resolved 211

The duck slaughtering industry and the chicken and duck industry have a dispute over the issuance of account payments in three-seven large and small foreign codes. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously convened both parties to discuss the issue, but the mediation failed because both parties held their own opinions. The association specially convened both parties again yesterday to re-mediate. Representatives from the Duck Slaughtering Operations Association Fang Xinpei, Weng Qiyin, Shen Xiaopin, Fang Luoji, Mi Xinda, and representatives from the Chicken and Duck Industry Association Yao Hanzhang, Zhang Lizhong, Ren Hongjun, Mao Zhongyu (represented by Jin Heqin), Zhang Xilin, Zhu Youhe, Wang Yuezhi, etc., were present. The mediation result was presided over by Yuan Hongjun, chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: (1) The record of the 7-3 foreign code decided by the Social Bureau in November of the 19th year of the Republic of China will be abolished from May 1st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. (2) From now on, duck slaughtering households will pay the industry account, all calculated at a 97% discount on the large foreign exchange (however, goslings will still be calculated at the old rules, at full foreign exchange), but in the future, when the government abolishes small foreign exchanges and implements subsidiary coins, accounts will be paid at full foreign exchange (3) Transactions between both parties are limited to members who have joined the same industry association. If the duck slaughtering households have not joined the Duck Slaughtering Operations Industry Association, the chicken and duck industry shall not trade with them. The same applies to chicken and duck industries that have not joined the Chicken and Duck Industry Association (the members of the same industry association of both parties are subject to the list notified by each association) (4) When goods are sold by the industry, they shall be collected as they are bought. If the peddler has a shortage of tail coins to find, it shall be cleared at the end of the month, and shall not be delayed. (5) When paying accounts, payment checks shall be paid. The maximum period is ten days. Small foreign exchanges shall be subject to market spreads, and shall not be arbitrarily raised or under pressure on market prices (6) Peddlers on both sides shall not trade privately (7) After these conditions are signed, if any member of either party violates them, the same industry association of each industry shall be responsible for supervising their implementation to avoid disputes. After the above mediation case was established, the representatives of both parties agreed to sign and record it for filing, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce presented it to the Social Bureau for replay, instructing both parties to comply.

Special Document

Overview of the Work of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration in the First Quarter of the 23rd Year 221

1. Introduction: Overview of the work in this quarter, from January 1st to March 31st of the 23rd year. At the beginning of the 22nd year, this bureau once revealed its policy outline, dividing the consolidation into active and passive parts, and the construction into spiritual and material parts. The work this year will continue to be carried out in accordance with this policy. The business of this railway is better in passenger transport than freight transport, and passenger transport is mostly third and fourth-class passengers, while freight transport is mostly less-than-carload freight. Therefore, the bureau's future consolidation and construction will pay special attention to promoting the business of third and fourth-class passengers and less-than-carload freight. The bureau has not been able to devote much effort to employee welfare undertakings in the past year due to the urgency of restoring business. This year, it plans to actively promote it.

2. Improving Administration: Implementing the standard weights and measures system, convening statistical meetings, and stipulating the method of compiling and publishing periodic reports.

Implementing the Standard Weights and Measures System 222

This railway has long implemented the standard weights and measures system, such as kilometers for the road line and kilograms for freight weighing. However, in other parts, most of them still use the inconsistent old Chinese system or the unscientific British and American systems. Since the National Government promulgated the Measurement Law of the Republic of China and stipulated a unified procedure, this railway is located in Jiangsu and Zhejiang and should have completed the unification before the end of the 20th year. However, due to various reasons, it has not been implemented. Then, the Shanghai Sino-Japanese Incident broke out, and the case was shelved again. In April of the 22nd year, an order was issued to select members from various departments to form a committee to prepare for implementation. At the same time, the engineering department compiled and printed a conversion table of weights and measures for backup. At the same time, all important drawings and material lists, etc., were revised and marked in meters by various departments, and the procedures were completed. Then, it was decided to completely switch to the new system from January 1st of the 23rd year and issued a general order for all departments to implement it uniformly.

Convening Statistical Meetings 223

Improving road affairs is based on statistics for more accurate comparison. In the past, the statistical work of the bureau was scattered in various departments, and the summary comparison was not enough to show the overall situation and exert its practical effect. Therefore, the general affairs department drafted various statistical tables, all using a monthly filling method, so that (1) when reference is needed in the middle of a year, the overall situation of each month can be obtained, and (2) after the end of a year, comparative statistical charts can be made to show the signs of its rise and fall. Then, it will be discussed with the relevant personnel of various departments on the method of supplying statistics every month, and the case of compiling the national statistical general report will be resolved together (to be continued).

Letter 224

To the Editor: We have read a news item in your newspaper's local news column about the import of Japanese sugar, which stated that more than 60 sugar merchants, according to a certain estimate, will have some sugar firms go bankrupt by the end of May. After checking, although the business of our industries has been sluggish and the profits have been meager due to the decline in people's strength last year, there are no families with huge losses. The closure of several companies in the first year was purely for other reasons. Now, the statement that several sugar firms will go bankrupt by the end of May is not known from what speculation. This is published, and it is inevitable that it is absurd, but it is very harmful to the credit and future of our industry. Please correct it quickly to avoid confusion. This is our sincere hope. Sincerely, Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, May 4th.

Reading Q&A

Questions After Reading "History of the New Chinese Literature Movement Materials" 226

(I continued)

- Answer to Mr. Wang Renkan -

The points raised in Mr. Wang's letter almost cover the entire new Chinese literature movement. If we want to answer in detail, we need a large work of 100,000 words. Now, we are limited by the length of this column. Although we strive for accuracy in our views, the development may not be exhaustive. This is what we want to ask Mr. Wang and all readers to forgive in advance.

To understand the literary achievements of the "May Fourth Movement," we must first understand the social significance of the "May Fourth Movement." Some old remnants of the "May Fourth" era often boast that the "May Fourth Movement" was launched by the "New Literature Movement." This statement not only aims to raise their own value and deliberately reverse the cause-and-effect relationship, but also hinders our fundamental understanding of the "May Fourth Movement." The "May Fourth Movement" is clearly an anti-imperialist and anti-feudal movement of the emerging national bourgeoisie. The result of the First World War made the European imperialists temporarily unable to take care of this colony, giving the national bourgeoisie a considerable opportunity for development. This aroused the consciousness of a part of the advanced bourgeois intellectuals on the one hand, but on the other hand, it threatened the emerging Japanese capital imperialism, making it have to take the opportunity to further attack China! The Twenty-One Demands for the destruction of China were put forward; the feudal warlords and bureaucrats surrendered. The "May Fourth Movement" inevitably broke out under these opposing circumstances. Social foundations were shaken, and the superstructure was shaken. Although the so-called New Culture Movement often manifested itself concretely before the actual movement, and although the development of the cultural movement was enough to promote the development of the actual movement, the success of the French Revolution did not rely entirely on Rousseau's call to "return to nature," but on the growth and strength of the French bourgeoisie itself. Using this to illustrate the "May Fourth Movement," we cannot say that the "May Fourth Movement" was launched by the "New Culture Movement." We should say that the "New Culture Movement" was launched through the "May Fourth Movement." If we do not grasp this point and do not start from a class perspective to understand the significance of the "May Fourth Movement" and the mutual relationship between the "May Fourth Movement" and the "New Culture Movement," we cannot solve the following problems.

What exactly did the "May Fourth Movement" achieve in literature? If we answer this question more concretely, we can say that it only raised questions and did not solve any problems at all, that is, there were no achievements. What Mr. So-and-so called "on the road to success" and "establishment" is a kind of self-deceiving exaggeration used to cover up his own escape, surrender, and weakness in running back to the old home of "organizing the national past." This reason, of course, does not blame Mr. So-and-so and similar intellectuals, but is determined by the fate of their class. The Chinese national bourgeoisie was cultivated by capital imperialism on the one hand and transformed by indigenous warlords and bureaucrats on the other. They are inherently characterized by comprador and feudal characteristics. Although they once stretched out their arms in the "May Fourth Movement" for the benefit of their own class, their undeniable timidity made them unable to last and unable to fight to the death. Once the struggle became sharp and their own interests were harmed, they would not hesitate to return to the arms of their old masters and willingly be slaves. This is reflected in the literary movement, and naturally there is no exception. Let's look at its achievements: From the beginning, the movement itself exposed many fundamental defects. First, the bourgeois intellectuals who led the movement did not have firm self-confidence and only regarded the movement as a "try." This can often be seen in the remarks of many gentlemen at that time. Therefore, they neither saw their future nor were willing to embark on their future. They were satisfied as long as they changed "zhī hū zhě yě" to "de me ne ma." Second, there was only the form of movement but no substantial content of movement. As far as vernacular is concerned, this was undoubtedly a weapon of assault for the national bourgeoisie to realize the two major demands of "science" and "democracy." Undoubtedly, it itself has a strong anti-imperialist and anti-feudal significance, but the leaders at the time only limited the problem to the discussion of the advantages and disadvantages of vernacular and classical Chinese, and could not attach more important social purpose consciousness, which caused it to completely stagnate in form. "De me ne ma" is used universally, but literary works containing struggle are ultimately not available. These two shortcomings cannot but be specially mentioned in examining the achievements of the literary movement at that time.

The result of the "May Fourth Movement" was to make the new literary movement! Or the vernacular movement, penetrated into the student and petty citizen strata of the petty bourgeoisie and expanded the influence of the new literary movement. This is a fact, but at the same time, the result of the May Fourth Movement further exposed the ugliness of those upper-class intellectuals, so they differentiated, wavered, and ended the life of their literary movement at this stage. Some of the more progressive elements among them took further direct action in politics, needless to say. The other part obediently retreated to their old home, which is what Mr. So-and-so and others call "organizing the national past." "Organizing the national past" can never be compared with the Soviet Union's acceptance of literary heritage. The Soviet Union's proposal to accept literary heritage was because the social foundation of the new literature was extremely strong and was based on the view of making this emerging literature reach its peak. Otherwise, why didn't they raise this question before the completion of the first five-year plan? Mr. So-and-so and others are clearly surrendering to the construction literature, avoiding the literary struggle in reality and hiding in a dead end. Textual research on Dream of the Red Chamber and blindly praising Awakening the World are not only of no help to new literature, but in fact, they are enough to help the tiger commit crimes, intentionally or unintentionally fulfilling the obligation of the feudal literary Mandarin Duck Butterfly School. This group of intellectuals had already left the camp of the new literary movement after the "May Fourth Movement." They have been buried by the times.

In addition, the only ones who can be our object of study are the neutral group wandering in the artistic palace (to be continued).

Records of the Faint Fragrance of Imperial Incense 227

- Original by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

From the above Q&A, readers may ask, then what qualifications are required to be a railway official under the rule of the Manchu Qing government? The answer is very simple. As long as you can buy it with money, you are qualified! As for how they can do it, as long as they have the means to live, it's fine. For example, my brother Xunling, he is acting as a railway supervisor: but what is he supervising? Not only do I not know, even he himself does not know! The reason why he was able to get this position was simply because he was a student who graduated from a certain military school in France!

On the surface, the Empress Dowager was not only often deceived by her courtiers, but also seemed to be deceived by the officials of the railway department. In fact, how could she not know? She just pretended not to hear it! Because these people were as incurable to her as all the tedious etiquette in the palace: it was what she had to endure. But I can make a judgment, based on my experience in the palace, the Empress Dowager can be said to know everything about the various characteristics of her officials, such as arrogance, vanity, and pretense, and knows them very accurately!

When we were watching her talk to Meng Fuxiang, we believed that there were only two thoughts in her mind at that time: one thought was to drive him out and never see him again: the other thought was to laugh at him in his face. But she also knew that if she really drove Meng Fuxiang away, the one who replaced him might be even more unbearable. Then laugh at him? ... No! Because the dignity of the Empress Dowager is what she has to maintain!

Because if we find something funny and want to laugh in our hearts, we only need to return to our own car and we can laugh out loud! (26)

Northeast Four Company Commanders 230

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 28: Coincidental Viewing, Foolish Passion for a Handkerchief, Earnest Inquiries About Illness, Misunderstanding Leads to a Letter

He returned home, and his elder brother and sister-in-law also returned from the city by car. He went to the main room, exchanged a few polite words with them, and at dinner, forced down half a bowl of rice. Then, he quietly returned to his study, propped his head on the table, and peeked out the window. Seeing no one passing by, he rummaged through his clothes for a while and pulled out a white silk handkerchief. On the corner of this handkerchief were embroidered two small osmanthus flowers and three green leaves, a diminutive representation of Yang Guizhi's name, indicating it was his private possession. He held the silk handkerchief, flipped it over, and examined it twice, then sniffed it several times, finding the fragrance intoxicating and filling his heart with a sense of joy. Because he felt so delighted, he held the handkerchief tightly, lost in thought. He savored the memory of how the handkerchief came into his possession. He remembered that when he dared not look at Guizhi any longer, Guizhi took out this handkerchief from her bosom and gently dabbed it on her face twice. Then, seemingly carelessly, she took the handkerchief back with her left hand and tucked it under her left arm. However, the opening of her dress was on the right, so how could she tuck it in on the left? Therefore, after several attempts, the handkerchief remained in her hand. It seemed her entire attention was focused on the stage, so she was completely unaware of what was happening with her own person. After a long time, her hand, perhaps out of absentmindedness, let the handkerchief fall onto the back of the chair, and she continued to watch the performance. He originally dared not touch her private property, but even after the performance ended, she didn't seem to notice the handkerchief. After she got up, he picked up the handkerchief. Looking at it this way, perhaps she intentionally passed the handkerchief to me privately, which is not impossible. If I didn't pick it up, I would be ungrateful for her kindness. Ji Zhi sat in his study, pondering layer upon layer, and the more he thought, the more he felt Guizhi's affection was profound. Originally, she was already married, and her father-in-law treated her with great kindness. How could she show disloyalty at this time? She probably knows how tormented I am, so in her helplessness, she used this handkerchief to comfort me. Actually, it would be better if she didn't comfort me at all, because this kind of comfort only plunges me deeper into the sea of love. (377)

The somewhat indifferent glance seemed to say, "You poor thing!" Conversely, arriving late demonstrates your busy schedule, thus increasing your value. If you can "barely warm the seat" before taking a sip of wine and excusing yourself, offering profuse apologies for having to leave due to too many commitments, and then hurriedly rush off, then your generosity and extensive social circle will undoubtedly leave a "delicious aftertaste" for the "nine brothers" at the "round table" to savor and admire.

Chinese people, living in such a hypocritical social environment, how can they talk about "punctuality?" Moreover, most of their watches tell different times, each going its own way. If the "time" isn't accurate, how can there be any "punctuality?" This reminds me of another joke about "imported goods."

A Westerner invited a friend who had once broken an appointment. Ten minutes after the appointed time, his friend finally arrived, looking nonchalant. He angrily questioned his friend about his chronic tardiness. The friend showed him his watch, intending to protest. After some debate and a thorough check, it was proven that the latter's watch was inaccurate due to a loose spring. So he said seriously, "Friend, would you rather keep our friendship or keep this watch?" To have the issue of a watch involve friendship, truly hilarious to Chinese people!

— Yuan Wenguang

Recently, I discovered that our Chinese characters themselves contain several special meanings. If you don't believe me, listen to me explain.

(1) 朝 (Chao - Dynasty/Morning): National Day - October 10th. (十月十日)

(2) 居 (Ju - To reside/Live): Mummy - Ancient corpse. (古屍)

(3) 踵 (Zhong - Heel): Flying legs - A thousand-mile foot. (千里足)

(4) 肉 (Rou - Meat): Self-proclaimed wife - Inside entry. (内入)

(5) 信 (Xin - Letter/Believe): Weekly magazine name - Human words. (人言)

(6) 共 (Gong - Together): Commemorative day of the Shanghai War - Japan - January 28th. (一二八)

(7) 孤 (Gu - Alone): Necessary item for entertaining guests in our society - Melon seeds. (瓜子)

(8) 轉 (Zhuan - To turn/Transfer): Special train - Special train. (專車)

(9) 捉 (Zhuo - To catch): Siblings - Hands and feet. (手足)

(10) 要 (Yao - To want/Important): Foreign woman - Western woman. (西女)

(11) 拾 (Shi - To pick up/Ten): Posture of chanting Buddha - Joining hands. (合手)

(12) 淼 (Miao - Vast expanse of water): County name in Guangdong Province - Sanshui. (三水)

(13) 甥 (Sheng - Nephew): Joy of having a son - Birth of a boy. (生男)

(14) 姓 (Xing - Surname): Joy of having a daughter - Birth of a girl. (生女)

Small Recipes

Talking About Salted Duck Eggs 234

— Zheng Yimei

Salted duck eggs are a very common food, and in the spring and summer seasons, they are especially good to eat with porridge in the morning. I remember a joke: "A certain son ate a salted duck egg and didn't know why. One day, he tasted salted duck and suddenly realized: 'So, salted duck eggs are laid by salted ducks!'"

Salted duck eggs made in Gaoyou are the most famous, commonly called Gaoyou eggs. When opened, this kind of egg is as red as amber and has oil flowing out. Its taste is rich and beautiful, incomparable. However, after being stored for a long time, the red turns black, with a different aroma, but many people still like to eat black yolk eggs. Moreover, those who wear black fragrant cloud gauze shirts and trousers with a white long gown are also called "black yolk eggs," a very apt comparison.

The Du method for making salted duck eggs involves mixing the brine from the year-end salted fish with rice straw ash, stirring it evenly, and then applying it to the washed fresh duck eggs. After about a week, they can be eaten. Some people also soak river sand in boiling salt water and apply it to the eggs, but it is not as rich and beautiful as the salted fish brine and rice straw ash. People in coastal areas all burn coal, and using coal ash as a substitute is even worse than river sand.

Salted duck eggs have a long history. Rong Zhai Sequel says: "The Jade Chapter and Tang Rhymes explain the character 杬 (yuan): a type of wood that grows in Yuzhang. Its juice can be used to preserve fruits and eggs without spoiling them. Exotic Things Records says: '杬 (yuan) means salted duck eggs, which are made by mixing the bark juice of the 杬 tree with salt.' Now, we have this everywhere in our hometown. It is like cocklebur and motherwort, not purely wood. When petty people fight, they take its leaves and rub them on the skin, causing it to turn red and swollen, falsely accusing their enemy of injury. As for preserving duck eggs, they also use it to dye the outside, making them look ochre in color."

A Note on Pig Blood Mushrooms 235

— Sun Zongtang

Hui Spring Mountain in Wuxi, with its nine peaks soaring high, surrounded by Tai Lake, boasts the beauty of springs, rocks, terraces, and pavilions. The mountain produces a type of mushroom called pig blood mushroom, which is fragrant, fresh, and tender, a unique style among wild mountain delicacies. It is a pity that few outside know about it and cannot taste this unique flavor.

Pig blood mushroom is a type of fungus, purple-red like blood, non-toxic, hence its name. Every year in April and mid-September, it grows among the pine firewood at the foot of Hui Mountain. Villagers from the mountain carry bamboo baskets to pick them. For one yuan, you can only buy a little over a pound, making the price quite expensive.

Pig blood mushrooms are best cooked with fresh bamboo shoots and bean curd, resulting in a delicious flavor, and the mushrooms are tender and pleasing. This dish is considered to be best prepared at a certain restaurant attached to the Jichang Garden in Hui Mountain. This garden is owned by the Qin family, and the Qing Emperor Qianlong once stayed there. Encircling Hui Mountain, with rippling waves and misty shadows, tall pines leaning over, and flying pavilions with flowing vermilion, it stands tall and majestic. If you want to taste this mountain delicacy, you can go to this garden, where, in addition to enjoying the special products of Hui Mountain, you can also admire the famous garden scenery, which is also a pleasure.

Cooking pig blood mushrooms with high-quality autumn oil, storing them in a ceramic jar, and using the oil to marinate tofu, which can be eaten with porridge in the morning, has a unique flavor, even better than shrimp roe soy sauce. Pig blood mushroom soup is extremely delicious and rich. All temples in Xiyi consider this a delicacy on their vegetarian banquets.

Also, pig blood mushrooms can be cooked with tofu skin, wheat gluten, and fresh bamboo shoots. Wheat gluten is a special product of Wuxi, rich in vitamins, which is beneficial for human nutrition.

In short, pig blood mushrooms should only be cooked with vegetarian ingredients to have a unique flavor. If cooked with meat dishes, they will taste bland.

Mr. Zheng Yimei, a literary giant of the Xing Society, is renowned at home and abroad for his literary sketches. Now, his book "Yimei Sketches" is being published, recording famous scholars and beauties, landscape scenery, and all kinds of birds, fish, and playthings, all of which are exceptionally elegant and witty. I received a copy yesterday and would like to express my gratitude.

Chinese Education Society Suggests to the Legislative Yuan Regarding the Constitution

It Should Be Stipulated That Education Funds Be Independent with a Minimum Percentage 260

The Chinese Education Society yesterday sent a letter to the Legislative Yuan suggesting that the Constitution should stipulate that education funds be independent, and that the word "minimum" should be added before the percentage, stating, "Respectfully submitted, we believe that education is a fundamental plan for establishing the nation. In this time of national decline and crisis, national revival and salvation depend on education. Whether education can develop depends on whether education funds can be independent and stable. Since the European War, all countries that have revived or rebuilt have generally established special chapters or articles on education in their constitutions, and many have made practical provisions regarding the sources and allocation of funds. Looking back at our country since the implementation of new education, there has never been a clear stipulation guaranteeing education funds. In recent years, foreign troubles have been frequent and internal disturbances have arisen from time to time. In fact, education funds have been affected by politics and military affairs, and there has been no stable situation. The misfortune of the country is also a crisis for education. Those engaged in education are compelled by enthusiasm and troubled by livelihood, and are trapped in a dilemma, with little way to be self-reliant or to help others. As a result, they change careers one after another and enter officialdom, which is common, and the national education suffers from it. It is difficult to revive and save the nation in this way. With this in mind, the Association resolved at its second board meeting to 'suggest to the Legislative Yuan that the special chapter on education in the Constitution should clearly stipulate the independence of education funds and guarantee that the percentage of education funds stipulated should have the word "minimum" added to prevent malpractices'. Therefore, we specially state the reasons, record the case, and send it to you, respectfully requesting that clear provisions be made in the special chapter on education in the Constitution to avoid the emptiness and disorder of education funds and to bring education to a healthy and stable state. This matter concerns national survival, and we hope that it will be adopted and implemented. We are eagerly awaiting this."

Students in Beijing Go to the Ministry of Education

Demanding Modification of Entrance Examination Regulations 261

(Nanjing Electric Dispatch, 4th) Twenty-one student representatives from private middle schools in Beijing went to the Ministry of Education on the afternoon of the 4th to petition for permission to modify the middle school graduation examination regulations, requesting two points: (1) The graduation rate should be considered to be above 95%, and the examination results should be calculated with school grades accounting for 60%; (2) The results of the examination should be released two weeks later, and failures and make-up examinations should be held within the third week. Dai Yingguan, section chief of the Ministry of Education, received them and said that the examination regulations were issued to all provinces and cities for uniform compliance, and it would be inconvenient to modify them in one place. If there are any opinions, they must first be submitted to the Beijing municipal education administration for verification.

Principal Huang of Qixia Declared Not Guilty: Lawyers Zhang Yipeng and Chuan Kuanglin Diligently Defended. The Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Federation Sent a Letter of Thanks 262

Huang Zhifu, Principal of the Jiangsu Provincial Qixia Mountain Rural Normal School, is enthusiastic about education, and the extension projects he runs are particularly beneficial to society. Because of this, he was wronged by a petty person, a monk named Jiran from Qixia Temple, who had a bad reputation and repeatedly made trouble for the school, falsely accusing the principal in the Jiangning Court. The court repeatedly rejected the accusations. Last year, the monk again framed Principal Huang in a criminal case, accusing him again in the Jiangning District Court, buying witnesses and colluding to fabricate confessions in various ways, to the point where Huang lost the case and was sentenced to imprisonment. Huang felt humiliated for no reason and refused to endure it, so he appealed to the Suzhou High Court and asked lawyers Zhang Yipeng and Chuan Kuanglin to defend him according to the law. People in the education community throughout the province also rose up to help, and the truth became clear. A few days ago, the High Court declared Huang not guilty. All the principals of secondary schools in Jiangsu Province admired lawyers Zhang Yipeng and Chuan Kuanglin for enthusiastically protecting education, speaking out for justice, reversing the case, and overturning the original verdict. Yesterday, Cao Chu, Zhang Haicheng, Liu Hengjing, Shao Heting, Wu Zhidi, Zheng Tonghe, and Zhou Houhu, seven executive committee members of the Middle School Federation, representing all the principals, sent a letter to lawyers Zhang and Chuan expressing their gratitude.

Principal Peng of Songjiang Middle School Describes the Student Unrest 263

Jiangsu Provincial Songjiang Middle School sent a letter saying, "To the esteemed editor of your newspaper: Recently, I read a report in the 'Education News' column of your newspaper on April 29th about the student unrest in the third grade of Songjiang Provincial Middle School, in which the students opposed the mid-term examination, claiming it was unnecessary. This is completely contrary to the Ministry's regulations and the school's rules. Article 2 of the school's temporary regulations on academic performance evaluation states that there is a mid-term examination, which has been approved by the Education Department with Instruction No. 12061 for reference. This method is not only commonly practiced in schools across the country for many years, but also is very consistent with the recent regulations of the Ministry of Education's middle school regulations, Article 51. It has been implemented for years without any objection. The Guidance Office scheduled the senior third grade mid-term examination to be held from March 26th to March 28th, arranged the schedule, and announced its implementation. Unexpectedly, the students of that grade only agreed to participate in the mid-term examinations for various elective courses, but refused the mid-term examinations for the three required subjects of Party Principles, Chinese Language, and English. When asked for their reasons, they had no answer. After repeated persuasion by the teachers of the Guidance Office and the class teachers, the grade sent a letter stating, 'The graduation trip of this grade is imminent. There is not enough time to prepare for the required subjects of this term. The completion of the elective courses is equivalent to a term examination. Students must fully prepare for credit purposes, so it is difficult to take care of the required subjects. We request that the Guidance Office change the arrangements and move the required subjects to after the spring break, which is convenient for both sides.' In view of this, the school did not reject their request for postponement.

I thought that from then on, it could be implemented on a regular basis. On April 18th, Wei Ji contacted the public affairs and asked for leave from the Education Department to go to Zhenjiang and then to Beijing. All school affairs were entrusted to the Deputy Director of Guidance Jiang Dongcheng. Then, the senior third grade mid-term examinations for Party Principles, Chinese Language, and English were scheduled to be held on the 22nd and 23rd of this month. According to the investigation, the students of that grade still refused, which was unreasonable. According to Article 57 of the Middle School Regulations, 'Students in the second semester of the third year of middle school may be exempted from the term examination, and the usual grades of each subject shall be used as the term grade.' If the grade's request is accepted and the mid-term examination is not held, the Chinese Language subject can be given credits according to the usual writing grades, but there is no way to calculate the scores for the Party Principles and English subjects. We are forced to ask the teachers to forge the scores, which not only destroys personal integrity, but also destroys educational administration. In fact, since there are no mid-term examination scores for these three subjects, there are no scores for the second semester of the third grade, and graduation cannot be allowed. This is why all the colleagues of the school insisted on the standard of the examination questions. Although special accommodation can be made, the mid-term examination is a must. Also, it is not true that a certain director saw a student sneaking out of the school one night and did not stop him on the spot. Wei Ji applied for leave from the Education Department on the 18th to go to Zhenjiang and then to Beijing. All school affairs were entrusted to the Deputy Director of Guidance Jiang Dongcheng. After lunch on the 19th, eleven senior third grade probation students, Tang Zeyi, Yu Shenrunmin, Huang Chaoguang, and students Cao Kongzhao and others, went to the theater without leave to seek entertainment. When the doorman tried to stop them, they lied and said they were visiting a certain meeting place. Later, after careful investigation by the Guidance Office, the truth was found out, and the students were confronted and confessed the truth. Colleagues in the Guidance Office felt that the situation was too serious to handle on their own. On April 24th, Wei Ji returned to school after completing the public affairs and handed it over to Wei Ji for verification. If entry and exit are free, school rules will inevitably be swept away. It is even more difficult to tolerate this kind of behavior occurring in the senior third grade. A meeting was immediately convened with the three directors of guidance, discipline, and affairs, the senior third grade teachers, class teachers, and other relevant personnel to discuss and decide to follow the Education Department's Instruction No. 252 on rectifying the academic style of the third grade, and to consider the students' previous academic performance in detail and to punish them separately by expulsion. The holding of the mid-term examination and the school rules are crucial and cannot be changed easily. The punishment of the students is deserved and not a harsh requirement. There are discrepancies between what your newspaper reported and the facts. Therefore, I specially request that you disclose the letter in order to correct it and avoid misunderstandings. I am very grateful for this." This is addressed to Mr. Editor-in-Chief of the Shanghai Shen Bao, Principal Peng Weiji.

Youth Worries and Health Education 276

(Two) (Zhou Shang)

(4) Health and Schooling. Almost everyone who can meet the requirements of schooling is not a few. Everyone thinks that the economy is the most important thing. In fact, the economy is still a secondary issue. It is not seen that many poor men with empty walls have succeeded in their studies since ancient times. Having no money does not necessarily prevent one from achieving academic success. Lacking wisdom is the fatal flaw in seeking knowledge. People who are unhealthy lack wisdom in nineteen out of ten cases. According to statistics, there is a great difference in the thinking ability and memory of unhealthy people and healthy people. You can understand by looking at these two tables (tables omitted). The table clearly indicates that only healthy people have excellent thinking ability, and only healthy people have excellent memory. Looking at the table on the impact of health on academic performance, the report shows that 50% of healthy people have excellent academic performance, 37% are of medium grade, and only 2% are listed as inferior. Conversely, among unhealthy people, 30 out of 100 are classified as inferior, and getting excellent grades is truly rare. According to a survey by L. WRapeer in the United States, 15% of students drop out due to physical problems, 16% repeat grades, and 17% are demoted. In this Shanghai municipal examination, many people fell ill and could not graduate. It is a pity that their efforts failed. Li Tingan, director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, has been studying health education for many years. He told me that his nephew had tonsillitis and his academic performance deteriorated, repeating grades for two years out of three. After he detected the cause and cured it, his academic performance improved by leaps and bounds. These are all true facts. This is something everyone should realize. Only with a sound body and mind can one have a sound mind. Remember this saying, and it will be of great benefit to your studies.

(5) Health and Occupation 277

The common perception is that money, machines, and land are the only capital for engaging in an occupation. However, the most important capital is not money, machines, or land, but our health. This is because health is the source of wealth. The American Labor Association estimates that industrial workers lose a total of 248 million days of work each year due to illness. Including losses in production, land resources, medicine, and other expenses, the total amounts to 772.85 million US dollars. The British Royal Commission estimates that illness is the cause of poverty for 55% to 66% of the national population. Western scientists say that the demise of Greece was due to disease, and the demise of Rome was also due to disease. China, known as the "Sick Man of East Asia," needs no further mention. According to our health statistics, the average mortality rate per thousand people is 15 in foreign countries, while it is 30 in our country. Out of a population of 400 million, 6 million people die unjustly each year. Shanghai's total population is 3 million, so the number of people who die unjustly each year is almost twice the population of Shanghai. If we calculate the economic loss, each person spends at least 50 gold coins per year on average. If they die at the age of ten, each person will have spent at least 500 gold coins, excluding medical expenses. For every 6 million people, there is a loss of 3 billion gold coins. With an annual expenditure of 3 billion gold coins, what can China not accomplish? Using this amount to develop construction projects, we could build 100,000 li of asphalt roads, 30,000 li of railways, 800 factories, 5,000 hospitals, 100,000 elementary schools, and 600 water plants. If we develop these projects every year, we won't have to worry about the lack of occupations.

Measuring Transformer Voltage Under Load 278

— Yi Zhi

Repairmen and experimenters often want to calculate the voltage of a power transformer under a certain load. This is actually easy. Anyone with a basic understanding of arithmetic can solve it using the following simple formula.

(1) E = e - cRRI + RE, where E is the transformer voltage under load RI.

R is the total AC impedance of the secondary coil. (A·C Impedance)

e is the voltage of the transformer without load.

Ri is the total AC impedance of the load.

Figure 1 AB

Figure 2 VA

How to solve this formula? As shown in Figure 1, the value of e, measured without load at point AB, is 620 volts. The value of R, measured with an ohmmeter for DC resistance, is 400 ohms. (Although this value should be measured at 60 cycles AC, the difference is slight and this error point has little impact.) The resistance RI is a voltage divider with a resistance of 6,000 ohms. What should the transformer voltage be when the load is 6,000 ohms?

Solution: Substitute the measured values into the formula, and the calculated result is approximately 300 volts.

This method can be used to calculate the current in rectifiers and the plate circuits of various vacuum tubes.

For step-down transformers, the coil resistance can also be accurately measured with an ohmmeter. (For large power transformers, use a Wheatstone Bridge to measure their DC resistance.) The formula is as follows:

(2) R = eEII, where I is the current, in amperes. Example: A radio has four vacuum tubes whose filament current requires four amperes. As shown in Figure 2, when using six vacuum tubes, requiring six amperes, what is the voltage drop after the filament voltage drops?

Solution: The voltage e without load is 2.7 volts, and the voltage E with load is 2.25 volts. Substitute these values into the following formula:

R = 2.72.25·454 = 0.112 ohms. Once R is obtained, the voltage drop after step-down at six amperes should be: (3) EIER E = 2.7 (6X0.112) E = 2.03 volts.

Improving Antenna Coupling 279

— Ming Li

If you want to make the tuning capacitors of a high-frequency amplification stage adjustable with a single shaft, the first difficulty is how to prevent the tuning circuit of the first high-frequency stage from being affected by the coupling of the antenna circuit and changing its wavelength range. Figure 1A shows the simplest tuning circuit. Its wavelength can be completely determined by the inductance of coil L1, the distributed capacitance, and the maximum and minimum capacitance of capacitor C1. The curve is uniform, as shown in Figure 2A. Now, use another coil L2 to replace the primary of an ordinary high-frequency transformer, so that it is coupled with L1 (Figure 1B). If L2 is open, the wavelength curve of C1 will not change at all. In actual circuits, for all high-frequency stages except the first stage, L2 is connected across the plate and screen grid of the previous high-frequency tube (Figure 1C). At this time, L2 and its associated circuits affect L1, increasing the inductance of L1, and the wavelength curve of C1 also becomes Figure 2B. Now, if the first high-frequency stage is to be adjusted with a single shaft, its wavelength curve must conform to B.

If the antenna is connected to this same primary coil L2, the effect of increasing the L inductance is even greater because the antenna inductance and capacitance are incorporated into the primary circuit. The three curves C, D, and E in Figure 2 represent the wavelength curves of C1 after connecting short, medium, and long antennas.

From this, it can be seen that the L2 of the first high-frequency stage cannot be the same size as the L2 of other stages. Therefore, this high-frequency transformer must be specially designed, but even if it is well designed, it can only be applied to antennas of a certain length. To avoid this difficulty, L2 can use the same type as other stages, but another capacitor C3 is connected in parallel with it (Figure 1E). Match this capacitor so that it is equal to the interelectrode capacitance of the high-frequency tube plate and screen grid. In this way, its wavelength curve can still be consistent with (Figure 2B).

This circuit also needs to be connected in series with a coil L3 (Figure 1E) so that it can be coupled with the antenna, and the capacitance of C3 must be reduced to maintain the original characteristics of this circuit. If the antenna is coupled to L3 through L4 (Figure 1G), because the variation of inductance is gradually weakened from one circuit to another, even if the variation of L4 is extremely large, the effect on L1 is extremely weak. Experimental results show that if the tightness of the coupling can be properly matched, the wavelength curve of C, no matter what the length of the antenna, will always be consistent with Figure 2B. The most perfect circuit is Figure 1H, because it has properly matched all the coils and C3 can be omitted. The capacitance between coil L3 and the ground wire is sufficient to replace it.

The advantages of the above antenna coupling method are three:

(1) It can make the capacitor of the first high-frequency stage and other stages into a perfect single-shaft adjustment.

(2) The structure of all high-frequency transformers can be exactly the same.

(3) Only by changing the degree of antenna coupling can the volume be controlled.

Appearance of Ultra-Short Wave Miniature Vacuum Tubes 280

— Bo Qing

In the past, when using vacuum tubes to receive ultra-short waves, the limit was about five meters. Above this, although special methods such as electronic oscillation could be used reluctantly, the operation was unstable and the sensitivity was poor, so there were many inconveniences in practical use. However, according to recent research, it is known that if a method can be found to keep a certain ratio between the two electrodes, the characteristics will not change regardless of how small the shape is. Even one that is about one-tenth of the current type can be used reliably even at ultra-high frequencies of 0.5 meters, and has actually been test-produced.

These two prototypes are heat-insulated triodes and screen grid tetrodes. The spacing between the electrodes is actually in units of 1/1000, so the degree of narrowness is really amazing. The characteristics are listed below:

A Very Good Two-Tube Radio Circuit 281

— Pan Yuxian

When we design radios, if we want to save a few vacuum tubes, we mostly tend to use regenerative circuits. However, although regenerative circuits perform well, many difficulties often occur in manufacturing and arrangement, often without good results. In the circuit below, detection is handled by a crystal detector, and its output (crystal output) is amplified by the control grid of the first vacuum tube, and then fed back into the detection circuit through the coupling of the screen grid coil; at the same time, their screen grids are also used for the first stage of low-frequency amplification. In form, it seems to be a regenerative circuit, but there should be no difficulty in manufacturing, and there is only one capacitor and moving coil on the panel, and the control is not complicated.

Coil L is the primary, and it is connected to L1 to increase sensitivity. L2 is the feedback coil, all wound on a spiderweb board. The primary is about ten turns (those using short antennas need to increase it), and the secondary is sixty or seventy turns, which must be determined by experimentation. If necessary, a tap can be added at point X for matching. Forty turns are enough for regeneration. The crystal can be fixed or movable. The resistance values of resistors R5 and R3 must be very accurate, otherwise it is easy to cause distortion. When using 135 volts for the B battery, a loudspeaker can be used. The bypass capacitor C6 must not be omitted. The remaining values are noted in the diagram, so I will not repeat them.
