The Past and Present of Vacuum Tubes (Continued) 286

— Manuscript from Philips Company

(2) Early Development: The specialized technology of radio vacuum tubes has progressed extremely rapidly. The reason for this should be attributed to the enthusiastic research of amateur home enthusiasts in various countries and the expansion of the army and navy. Moreover, the need for good quality and inexpensive radios by the public has promoted the development of specialized technology, and the manufacturing of vacuum tubes has become increasingly perfect.

At the same time, the D-series tubes produced by Philips are undoubtedly a great achievement. Although their reception is weaker, it does not matter. On the one hand, the extremely heavy B battery has been reduced as much as possible due to the emergence of low-vacuum tubes and dual-grid tubes. The only fly in the ointment is that each tube still requires a large current of 0.5 amps. If a four-tube machine is turned on for five hours a day, the large-capacity battery will be exhausted within a few days, which is not economical.

Therefore, micro-heat tubes came into being to meet the needs of the times. Almost all the tungsten filaments used in old-fashioned vacuum tubes were eliminated and replaced with barium oxide-coated filaments. Because barium oxide can emit a larger amount of electrons at low temperatures, the current consumed in this new type of vacuum tube is extremely small, about one percent of the current consumed in old-fashioned vacuum tubes. The manufacture of micro-heat tubes began in 1923 (AI06 and A306). A few years later, high-voltage vacuum tubes began to appear on the market to compete with low-voltage tubes, prompting scientists to focus on the design of special vacuum tubes (to be continued).

Recent Radio Miracles 287

— Shi Huayu

Among the various scientific inventions in the twentieth century, radio is probably the most amazing, right? Imagine, day and night, countless radio stations emit radio waves that intersect and pass through our bodies, but we don't feel anything. Music, speech, SOS signals for help, alarms, etc. constantly invade your body within 24 hours a day. Isn't this amazing enough? If you use a very sensitive radio, you can feel all these thousands of radio waves of all shapes and sizes all over the world. As for the radio waves themselves, unless we are experts, we don't understand them very well. In fact, radio waves are the same as light waves. For example, the speed of light waves is 186,000 miles per second, and so is the speed of radio waves. However, light waves are what our visual organs can feel, while radio waves require special sensing devices.

Through the continuous research of engineers and scholars in the world, miracles have emerged one after another. When Heinrich Hertz

Page 16

first experimented with the induction coil and the spark gap, the radio waves generated were like a stone thrown into water, creating some water waves that disappeared in an instant. A few years later, when the vacuum tube was invented, the full wave appeared. Later, scientists used it to add another frequency of radio waves (such as audio frequency), and the amplitude modulation effect was successful. This is like a cork floating on a water wave, the water holds the cork, sinking and floating, and spreading far away. Thus, the radio telephone was produced.

Later, American engineers, because there was a disadvantage of not being able to keep secrets in transatlantic radiotelephones, came up with a method called inverted or scrambled speech. The principle of this method cannot be explained in this short article, but roughly speaking, it uses two oscillators to emit two different frequencies at the same time. Therefore, a special device must be used in the radio, otherwise what is received is just some vague sounds.

These are not considered strange! The strangest thing is that, according to recent news from Europe, someone has already invented a method that can broadcast two different programs from the same radio station, using the same frequency, at the same time, and can be mixed some. At the same time, engineers at Columbia Broadcasting Station in the United States have also successfully experimented with broadcasting television and speech simultaneously using one frequency. However, the radio must also have a special device. The principle is that two different programs use a local oscillator in the transmitter to make it work intermittently. In other words, it is using a paralyzing grid bias to connect two different low-frequency amplifiers to the same amplitude modulator. Since this amazing discovery, the opportunity for radio stations to broadcast can be doubled. However, can it only be doubled? I'm afraid it's not just that in the future. In wired telegraphy, isn't there a method called multiplex telegraphy? It can send as many as eight telegrams at the same time. So, in radio, if you continue to work hard, in the future, let alone eight, I'm afraid a dozen telegrams can be broadcast simultaneously under the same

frequency. The current smoky broadcasting situation in Shanghai may also get a solution from this!

A Radio with a Loudspeaker Using Only One Vacuum Tube 288

— Yong Yan

This radio uses only one vacuum tube and can play a loudspeaker, and the sound it produces is not to be called weak. Stable reception and simple adjustment are its characteristics. There is no difficulty in manufacturing and using it. If you pay a little attention when manufacturing it, it will definitely not fail.

The circuit output by this radio is the Flewelling super regenerative type, which uses a single No. 33 pentode strong amplification vacuum tube for detection. Its circuit is as shown in the attached diagram, and the component values are as follows:

C1 0.0005 variable capacitor. C2 C5 0.00025 Farad mica fixed capacitor.

C3 C4 0.0006 Farad mica fixed capacitor.

RI 1 million ohm grid leak resistor. RI 15 ohm variable resistance resistor. WI WI is wound on a one-inch diameter circular tube. WI is 110 turns of 32-gauge enameled wire, and W2 is 45 turns of 36-gauge double-silk wrapped wire.

Vacuum tube No. 33. (No. 83 and No. 47 can also be used)

A battery, 2 volts. B battery, 90 to 135 volts.

If it is not working after it is made, you can try switching the two-wire ends of W2. This machine does not need a ground wire. If you want to use a ground wire, connect it as shown by the dotted line in the diagram. Adding a fixed capacitor of 0.0001 Farad at the wiring nail of the loudspeaker can sometimes improve performance, you can try it. (The connection method is as shown by the dotted line in the diagram)

The fixed capacitors in this machine must be of the values specified, and they must all use mica insulation, so as not to reduce the regenerative power. The loudspeaker used should use a higher impedance, then the performance will be better. An antenna of 75 feet is sufficient, any longer than this may reduce

performance.

B-Class Detection Experiment 289

— Pan Yuxian

We all know that the output of Class B amplification is extremely strong, so it is very suitable for use in the final amplification stage. As for using it in the detection stage, it is still rare. The reason is that most ordinary radios that need very high sound waves tend to think about the low-frequency amplification section; and it is also very difficult to use two vacuum tubes in practice, but now that dual tubes have appeared, you might as well try it. Below is a standard circuit for Class B detection. The figure has a regenerative effect, so its effectiveness is no less than that of ordinary two or three-stage high-frequency amplification, and it can also be modified into a small-power transmitter. The manufacturing is also not very difficult.

Coil L is the primary, the number of turns is the same as ordinary ones, and each upper and lower part of LI2 is about one-half of the ordinary screen grid coil. For example: if the entire LI is seventy turns, then LIA is thirty-five turns, and LIB is also thirty-five turns, but its exact number of turns must be determined by experiment. GL is the grid leak. When the vacuum tube V uses dry electricity, ro can be used, and AC can use -53 and 2B6. Those who are interested in research should try it.

Free Talk

Village Gleanings (4) 291

— Feng Zi

(4) Impromptu Scene

The weather is getting warmer day by day, and the willow leaves in the yard are hanging like silk threads. The morning sun shines on the paper windows, making them feel warm.

Because I have to go out for a walk every day, I get up around six o'clock. This is not considered very early in the countryside. The earliest ones should be the sparrows in the eaves, whose chirping can be heard as soon as dawn breaks. Birds have an urgent need for light, and because their perches and flight paths are high, they have the quickest sense of light. Next are beasts, and humans are the slowest. This is because some people know how to take advantage of the darkness, while others succumb to it. As darkness becomes a habit for humans, the sense of light becomes duller day by day.

But among humans, there are differences. Poor people sense light faster than rich people, and rural areas faster than cities. This place is both rural and full of poor people, so as soon as the birds and animals chirp, people start moving in the breaking dawn. My daily destination is along the road north of the village. From that place, you can see the red glow as the sun rises in the east, and the chimneys of the farmers' houses curling around the elm trees behind the village. The air is filled with fragrance, and there are patches of purple alfalfa, tender green buds holding dew, and yellow rapeseed flowers.

In the gardens planted with cabbage and clover, groups of three or five young village girls squat there picking flowers. They plan to take them to the town to sell, which can bring in a good amount of money each year. Planting grain, planting wheat, planting every drop of the farmers' sweat, and bringing them to the city results in surprisingly low prices, and no one ever praises them. But if they bring flowers to the town, the ladies will say they are beautiful and fresh, and maybe they will even give a few extra coins when they are in a good mood.

Country people understand this situation very well, so the number of people growing flowers is increasing year by year, adding a lot of beautiful scenery to the countryside. This scenery also reveals a tragic fate.

The road north of the village is endless. I know how to stop my steps and stand watching the farmers working in the fields. They are busy loosening the soil, busy removing weeds. Their work is intense, and I really don't believe I have a reason to stand idly by.

Ladies, misses, masters, and young masters know how to enjoy those flowers, grains, wheat, and all kinds of novelties and foreign goods that country people can't even imagine. Luxury, debauchery, leisure, and enjoyment encompass their entire lives.

However, there is no reason for anyone to stand idly by.

Occasional Thoughts 292

— Anahan

Material things are finite, but the spirit is infinite. -- No matter who it is, the mention of Gandhi always inspires some reverence.

Indeed, before such a great personality, one cannot help but feel one's own insignificance and smallness. Emerging from death into life, dedicating one's entire soul to the nation, not suffocating oneself in the whirlpool of power, wisdom, deceit, and violence, but compassionately caring for all mankind, planning for their liberation, and envisioning the future: while not only seeing through one's own life and death, but also seeing through history, seeing through the world, and seeing through material things -- has there ever been such a great figure in the history of the East and West? This is why he is Maharama, Mahatma!

But Mahatma does not want people to honor him as Mahatma. He considers himself humble, believing that the great one is a heavenly god, God. A few years ago, when leading his followers to the seashore to collect salt, some followers walked in front carrying fire bowls. When Gandhi found out, he gave a long speech, believing that this was a humiliation for their followers, and he vowed: if our followers harass the people and receive offerings from them, it is no different from looting the people. Moreover, if that is the case, after we die, dogs will lick our bones!

Often rising before dawn, guided by the stars, to spin and weave, writing in his diary under the moonlight, giving speeches during the day, and handling affairs, all for the sake of saving the Indian nation and resisting the Europeans, yet strong, brave, and peaceful!

However, recently after being released from prison, he was attacked by thugs. Although he was not hit, several attendants were injured. What is the motive of these thugs who act as pawns for foreigners? It's like sitting on a tree branch and chopping down the trunk with an axe! But tens of millions of Gandhians will become angry and destroy everything. The British have always protected Gandhi, not because they didn't want to get rid of him, but because they feared something. But this is not the true heart of the Mahatma, who instead said: if my followers have done something wrong, I will repent!

Alas! This is the compassion of the world's greatest personality. Because of peace, he is broad-minded; because he seeks the liberation of mankind, he stands tall like a bright star in the sky, understood and worshipped by people all over the world. -- With this, one can measure the size and height of popular leaders of the past and present!

The Enemy 293

— Translated by Ling Yang from Bａrｄ—ｌａｉｒｅ

My youth was just a dark storm, with only a few rays of brilliant sunlight shining through from time to time. The few remaining crimson fruits in my garden, devastated by thunder and rain.

·······················

Now my heart has reached autumn,

I am waiting to use iron shovels and hoes to renovate the land that has been eroded into a tomb-like shape by floods.················· Who knows, can the flowers I dream of find the nourishment they need to grow in this sandy soil?············· Ah, misfortune! Ah, misfortune! Time devours life, and the enemies that erode our hearts and suck our blood are growing stronger and stronger.

Lujiang Dam 294

— Liu Ming

On the journey in western Yunnan, the most poisonous miasma place is probably Lujiang Dam. According to common lore, to pass through there, one must get up early in the morning, put a grass cigarette in the mouth, and quickly walk through. At other times, the miasma comes out. If you don’t know and venture out, and smell a sweet aroma like glutinous rice, that is extremely dangerous. When Yang Sheng'an was banished to Yongchang, he wrote a poem "The Precious Well," which included lines such as "Lujiang's eight bends have much miasma," and "The silent miasma has no cure." This shows that the frightening nature of Lujiang has been known since ancient times. However, this is only limited to the summer and autumn seasons. Winter and spring are not so serious. When I arrived there, luckily it was February, so I didn't have to choose a time or hold a cigarette in my mouth. I even stayed by the river for a night.

Lujiang Dam is a long and narrow plain along the Lujiang River (also known as the Nujiang River), flanked by high and steep peaks. The outside wind is very difficult to blow in, so it is very hot all year round. The cogon grass growing in the dam is stronger than elsewhere, which is probably proof of the toxic climate. There is an iron chain bridge on the river, connecting merchants between Yongchang and Tengyue. During the day, people and horses passing by may make it lively, but at night it lies there lonely, the river rushing and roaring below, rushing towards the mountain canyons to the south. On the plaque at the bridgehead, illuminated by the moonlight, the large characters "Lushui" were visible, along with a line of small script by Li Genyuan.

"Could the Lushui river where 'in the fifth month, crossing the Lu, going deep into barren lands' be this river?"

Harboring gloomy doubts, dragging my tired legs, I quickly stepped into the lit house under the bridge. But the men and women in the house who greeted me with surprised eyes were not like our Han people. The women wore short clothes that reached their abdomen and long skirts that reached their ankles, all in black. When they spoke, they revealed their black teeth, but their faces were beautiful. Their heads were wrapped in black silk, piled up to about a foot high, as if they were wearing a small bucket. As soon as I saw it, I couldn't help but think of the local ghosts in the City God Temple in my hometown. Moreover, the wind that sneaked in through the bamboo wall cracks blew the lights flickering from time to time, combined with their shadows running around the house barefoot, always made people feel a little scared. We had dinner at the same table with them. The rice was all cold, and the soup made of fern leaves and wild mushrooms, as well as the fried dried bamboo shoots, were only lukewarm. (The reason is that they don't like hot food, which is due to the hot weather). If you regard this night's experience as being in the underworld, it may be more appropriate. This was the first time I met the Baiyi people in western Yunnan.

Of the things brought to China by Westerners, the most common and deeply rooted in the interior is probably opium, which is second to none. The Baiyi people here have also long accepted this gift. When the hostess led me into another room to rest, a Baiyi teenager lying on a bamboo bed smoking a pipe slightly raised his head and greeted me, and looking at his delicate face, only fifteen or sixteen years old, made me feel a little gloomy.

"Tonight an old Han Chinese came to our old Baiyi's house!"

I heard the woman laughing in the next room, speaking stiff Yunnan dialect in a low voice, and also specially added two unnecessary "old" words. I smiled slightly as I took off my clothes, and I felt in my heart:

"This is a peaceful and kind nation!"

The Vast Sea 295

— Shu

This collection of letters is different from ordinary selections. The main feature is that it preserves many Ming Dynasty letters that have been lost or are now rarely seen. Second, it is not like Wang Shizhen's "Pure Selections of Letters," where the Ming Dynasty only occupies one volume, only one-sixteenth of the whole; nor is it like books such as "Ming Sages' Remaining Letters," which only select large articles discussing morality, making people's heads ache, but only some casual, very rhythmic lyrical essays, which are easiest to see the author's real life and true feelings. Third, although the selected letters focus on the Ming Dynasty, there are many from the late Ming Dynasty, especially those from the Gong'an School, which can be said to be very important documents for those who study this school of literature. In my subjective view, this book, compiled by Ming people, and Mei Gong's "Paired Fish Letters" can be called twin jewels.

Four

Among the Ming people, Wang Shizhen, Li Yu-lin, Chi Shui, Chen Mei-gong, and the three Yuan brothers collected the most letters, followed by Xu Wenchang, Zong Zixiang, and Lu Shen. Wang, Li, Xu, Zong, and Lu aside, Chi Shui's letters, although similar to his other writings, are not lacking in the disgusting atmosphere of parallel prose, but there are quite a few good ones. He said to Wang Baigu, "I am poor to the bone, and I don't want to frown at the butchers and wine sellers, so I open my mouth and laugh every day with joy. If I have a little money at home, I sit idly with relatives and friends for pure joy. When the mood strikes, I sing Xingqu, with young boys blowing pipes and playing Sheng beside me, which is very pleasant. The jars are empty, and the kitchen has no breakfast, but my spirit is still clear and bright. To end this life in this way is not bad." In a short passage, one can imagine his life and free and easy demeanor. Like other letters describing mountain life, he said, "Being in the present, I never calculate tomorrow's food, clothing, marriage, or household matters." As for Chen Mei-gong, the most letters in this collection are his. Difficult to abridge, some are no longer letters, but most are lovely chapters. I especially like to read his letter to Wang Yuanmei: "Since we parted, I have spent the spring in reading, not knowing that there are wine cups and flowers outside the door. I often remember the Qiyuan Temple, the green grass and singing birds; recently following your footsteps, laughing and talking in harmony. Such a beautiful scene has suddenly fallen into a dream!" And to Wu Dacheng, he said, "I spent more than two months avoiding the heat in Dongting Lake, with tall pines blocking the sun and flying waterfalls like snow. I eat dozens of loquats and bayberries every day. I regret that I cannot share them with you." Sending to a friend, he said: "From spring to summer in a Gengshen year, the old rain does not stop. The scenery in the mountains changes in a hundred ways, which is really enjoyable for the elderly. I often think of the Nan Guan father and son, still living in a painted world, not as good as our family's windy and rainy days, all of which are my painted forests. I should show it to Xuanzai and ask him to title it 'Talking about Rain.'" Written casually, in a few words, it really makes people linger. However, this is not the world we live in today.

Mud 296

— Ye Cangcen

In the twilight of a rainy summer day, I walked through a muddy path. Lush willow groves shaded both sides of the road, and passionate songs came from the grove.

I know that this is the singing of the orioles --

Fiery passion floating in the air!

Ah, my heart is also full of boundless passion. I want to turn it into a lingering new song; in the depths of silence, hide myself and pour out the same song as you! But alas, time does not allow me to stop for a moment, I must pass through the mud in front of me.

Shanpu Lottery (2) 297

— Tang Xiru

Inside the door: The blue gas lamp laughed hissingly. Millions of rays of light fell like rapid rain on the walls, tables, ground, and people. Further in, there was a high counter, like a pawnshop or a bank. The counter was surrounded by copper railings, on which were pasted many colorful paper slogans. On the left wall of the entrance hung two blackboards, on which were written in white powder the winning numbers from the previous draw. Many people wearing wooden clogs, armed belts, glasses, and slicked hair were constantly squeezing in and out of the shop's entrance.

Afa wanted to step in, but his legs just twisted to the side and then straightened out again, going back to the road he had come from. "So many people are buying, how can I win? It's harder than finding a needle in the sea! Hard! Hard! Hard! Don't be fooled!" His mouth was reluctantly arguing with his uncooperative feet.

Afa really didn't want to buy! If that's what he said, Afa's heart would protest. He really wanted to, but he couldn't help but feel a little flustered. He understood that it was his first time taking a train, his first time running into a big tea house, and he inevitably felt unnatural and flustered about every strange and novel thing.

It was really strange that in the rice fields in June and July, which were so hot that even the leeches were hot, his feet had never been as afraid to step into this shop as they were here.

"Be brave! This isn't stealing, what's there to be afraid of? Maybe there aren't any acquaintances there! So many people are pouring in and out, you can't recognize them all, and even if you do, what's there to be afraid of? It's not like I'm breaking the law. Besides, who doesn't love money? Who doesn't covet windfall riches? ········"

The louder the voice in his heart shouted, the faster his steps moved forward.

"Top-quality Luogang Dong glutinous rice lychees! ··· Two cents a catty." He had already reached the corner of Kuai Fu Street. He subconsciously took out a few copper coins and bought a few, peeling and eating them while turning back.

With lychees to peel and eat in his hand, others wouldn't suspect that he was intent on buying Shanpu lottery tickets. His courage had increased a lot. He lingered at the entrance for a while. He had to take a closer look at the shop.

At the door was a long red cloth banner with melon-sized gold characters: "Two cents can get you more than 40,000 yuan!" His heart shrank, and his blood stopped. Then it started to race and jump wildly. More than 40,000 yuan? He had only vaguely known before that winning the first prize could bring a lot of money, but he had never expected such a great joy. His feet stepped forward again. Ah, ah, no wonder they want to buy, ··· they are not stupid! Spending two cents to get more than 40,000 yuan, who says it's not worth it? Ah, ah, a thousand yuan is worth it, ten thousand yuan is worth it! ··· He walked to the fifth perfume shop and then turned back.

Let's go back and see what else is written in the shop.

A red piece of paper on the copper railing was blown by the wind:

"Hit it with a lucky hand!" His heart shook again, and his feet wanted to move forward again. No, wait a moment, let's see what a few more say. The second one, in yellow: "Buy it and win!" The third one, in blue: "Open the road to windfall riches!" The fourth one, in purple: "··········"

Financial: Silver Prices Rise; Speculation Fund Drops Ten Dollars and Five Cents; Thomas Amendment Postponement Keeps Market Stable; Cantonese Banks Liquidate, Breaking the Forty-Dollar Barrier 298

Yesterday, the gold market saw a rebound in silver prices. News of the recovery, which had been telegraphed and published the day before, had a wearying effect on foreign exchange sentiment. A wave of selling ensued, with Cantonese speculators liquidating their positions, leading to a volatile market that briefly broke through the forty-dollar barrier. Initially, overseas silver markets showed gains, with both British and American markets rising. The forward silver price on the Five Metals Exchange rose by varying degrees, from 3.5% to 6.6%. Exchange rates also increased. London raw gold fell by 3.5 pence, American cotton fell by 8 points, and American wheat fell by .625. The market opened sharply lower. Later, it breached the fifty-dollar barrier. However, a Reuters report stating that the Grace Amendment proposed by Senator Thomas, originally scheduled for discussion at a meeting between silver advocates and the President on Saturday afternoon, had been postponed to the following Monday, led to a rally that pushed prices back above the fifty-dollar mark. Subsequent Reuters dispatches were inconsequential. The HSBC Bank exerted significant effort to control both British and American exchange rates, stabilizing the silver market. With no high expectations, large investors began selling off positions, pushing prices below the fifty-dollar mark again. Later, the internal market softened, with arbitrage traders actively selling, and Cantonese banks such as Shengda and Hengxing also cutting their long positions. With banks tightening their lending policies, the gold market weakened further, dropping below the forty-dollar mark again. At noon, the market slightly stabilized as the Central Bank intervened with cash. The subsequent market performance was lackluster. In the Seattle night market, silver prices rose, experiencing a brief period of high-to-low volatility. Similar arbitrage transactions were not as active, leading to some market tightening and continued price increases internally. However, with Cantonese banks resuming sales, there was continued struggle. Ultimately, market sentiment stabilized as large investors bought in and old news resurfaced, such as the silver meeting being postponed to the following Monday. The market closed relatively stable. The Unfavorable State of Silk, Tea, and Spring Silkworms 314

"Zhejiang" Local Silkworm Breeds Undergoing Changes: In the four townships of "Haining," farmers raising local breeds account for forty to fifty percent. After hatching, the weather became abnormal, with a lingering spring chill, resulting in uneven ant emergence. The weather turned sunny and warm during the first molt, and development was satisfactory. However, after the second molt and leaf opening, alternating rain and sunshine brought cold weather, reducing the silkworms' resistance. Many experienced loss of sleep and stopped feeding. The development of improved silkworm breeds was also poor. Some failed to molt for the third time, while silkworms in the late second molt, which were consuming large quantities of leaves, also showed slow feeding. Efforts are now being made to isolate them and adjust temperature and humidity to prevent transmission. "Xiaoshan": Among the various towns and villages, the model district in the eastern region has the best silkworm season this year, with eighty to ninety percent raising improved breeds. Due to cold weather and heavy rain, the silkworm season is delayed. In recent days, continuous overcast and rainy weather with cold temperatures has caused silkworms in the early third molt to remain dormant for over thirty hours without seeking food. Everyone is increasing the temperature with stoves.

"Suzhou" Juvenile Silkworm Development Delayed: "Yixing" This year, silkworm farming in areas such as Li Du, Song Du Nan, Fufeng Bridge, Baojia Village, Xushe Qingbaili, etc., is relatively thriving, and many are raising improved breeds. However, due to the cold weather, development is poor. Hatching takes fourteen to fifteen days to begin, and mulberry buds produce leaves late. The early batches are currently in the second molt, while the late batches are opening leaves for six or seven days. Continuous rain has prevailed, and temperatures are low, with instances of sleep loss and cessation of feeding. "Changzhou" This year, fewer silkworm eggs are being raised in the northwest townships. Many are raising local breeds, and egg collection is uneven. Early batches are opening leaves for five or six days in the first molt, while late batches are also trying leaves. Recent rainy and overcast weather, coupled with cold temperatures, has led to many early silkworms suffering from diarrhea and dying after consuming rainwater-soaked leaves. In the eastern townships of Henglin, etc., the development of foreign silkworm breeds is slow due to the cold weather. Early batches are opening leaves for the first molt, while late batches are still just emerging. In the past two days, rain has been a problem, but fortunately, the impact on young silkworms is still minimal. However, the silkworm season is expected to be later than in previous years.

Qimen Black Tea Officially Opens Its Gardens 315

Qimen black tea, which in previous years would have been more than halfway through its harvesting and processing by this time, is experiencing difficulties this year due to the excessively cold weather. Even the tea buds on sun-facing tea trees in the plains have struggled to grow long. Consequently, tea estates that initially planned to start weighing tea on time have temporarily suspended operations. Only the tribute tea green tea from Shanli and Likou, etc., had a small harvest in the previous week, but the output was limited. The purchase price at the tea estates was approximately one yuan and forty-five cents per catty. In the past four or five days, the weather has shown signs of warming, and tea buds are flourishing. However, due to torrential rain day and night, mountain households have been unable to harvest and process the tea. Today (the 29th), the weather suddenly cleared up, and tea farmers in production areas such as Likou, Lunkeng, Taoyuan, Zhukou, Shanli, Gaotang, Penglong, Chentiankeng, Tafang, Pingli, and Guixi, etc., are taking advantage of the sunny weather to spread the tea leaves for drying. They are officially opening their gardens, focusing on tender leaves and discarding old ones to meet this year's standards. Various tea businesses are also sending people to the production areas to procure tea. Weighing is expected to begin in full force tomorrow or the day after. If the weather remains sunny and warm for a week, the first batch of tea produced is expected to be of excellent quality. However, the atmosphere in the production areas has become tense, and tea businesses are anxious. It is unlikely that mountain prices will be lower than in the past.

Ping-Shui Green Tea Gradually Entering the Market 316

Ping-Shui green tea produced in various cities and towns in Zhejiang province has recently begun to be harvested. New products from Zhuji, Xiaoshan, Xinchang, Yuyao, Lin'an, Shangyu, and other places have all entered the market. However, due to the cold weather, tea buds are developing slowly, and output is not particularly abundant. Consequently, various tea businesses are facing a situation of "more monks than porridge" when purchasing tea. The selling price of raw tea is approximately seventy-four to seventy-five yuan for top-quality tea and about sixty-six yuan for lower-quality tea, which is six or seven to ten yuan higher than in previous years.

Grain: Late Indica Rice Softens Slightly 318

Starch Market in a Spin 319

Yesterday, the starch market remained in a spin on both the upper and lower markets. At the opening of the market in the morning, the price of foreign wheat fluctuated. However, shorts, seeing the authorities' and manufacturers' determination to maintain prices, dared not fail to cover their positions to prevent a future short squeeze. Demand for stockpiling was also good, so prices for all months rose by about one cent at the opening. Subsequently, a major player dumped long positions in the current month, and a manufacturer hedged by receiving near-term and delivering deferred positions, causing the current month to fall immediately. Deferred months initially followed slightly, but after being bought by short hedges and absorbed by outside stockpiling, the market recovered. However, actual sales were sluggish, and inventories of spot starch were high, making a turnaround in the current month difficult. At the close, the price for the current month was down a half-cent, the next month was up 0.75, July/August were up 1 cent, September was up 1.25 cents, and October was up 0.75 cents.

Shen Bao Shanghai Local Supplement

Essays

Justice and Peace 322

-- Wen Li

"You say you're right, she says she's right" – this applies to individuals. This country says it advocates justice and peace, and that country says it advocates justice and peace – this is from the perspective of the nation. Individuals have different interests, so they argue and fight. Nations have conflicting interests, so they argue and start wars. But when individuals have different interests and hold different reasons, most people understand. But when nations have conflicting interests and advocate justice and peace, most of them keep their people in the dark and use them as cannon fodder. The magic of the slogan of justice and peace is therefore incredible.

According to a report by the Tokyo Telegraph Agency on the 2nd, Foreign Minister Hayashi and Army Minister Araki explained in detail to the Soviet Ambassador to Japan that the Japanese people have no intention of using force at any time. The military preparations Japan needs are within the extent to which the security of the Japanese Empire feels unthreatened. For the sake of justice, Japan is prepared and determined to resist, no matter the sacrifice. It was also emphasized that the world's claim that Army Minister Araki is a warmongering general is entirely due to a lack of understanding. Minister Araki is fundamentally a proponent of peace. – Such statements by proponents of justice and peace, when viewed in light of their years of military aggression in China, are the exact opposite. However, they believe that they are advocating justice and peace, which is worth discussing.

From the perspective of international warfare, when strong countries prepare and wage war to compete for markets, Country A inevitably takes preemptive measures to forcibly seize the territory of neighboring weak nations or countries as preparation to confront Country B, Country C, etc. However, no matter how eloquent you are, this behavior is always ironclad evidence of injustice and a lack of peace for the weak clans and countries whose territory has been seized. Since Japan has already seized our four northeastern provinces, it now declares that it advocates justice and peace. Where is the justice? Peace is even more nonsense. The authorities in our China should protest, but they are attempting to rely on other strong countries to extend justice and are shouting about the "Nine-Power Treaty." It is no wonder that an editorial in a certain newspaper said that China's demise lies in the Japanese minister's declaration that "China must not be interfered with." This is another matter. Just looking at Hayashi Araki's so-called advocacy of "justice" and "peace," his so-called "justice" is from the perspective of the Japanese Empire to maintain their interests, and his so-called "peace" is also to maintain their country's interests in East Asia. The interests mentioned here, are they not the interests of the entire Japanese people? The answer is no. The so-called "national interests," in the view of Japan, are probably the interests of a minority who benefit from competing for overseas markets.

Only a country that is being bullied, oppressed, and invaded is qualified to advocate justice and peace from the perspective of the nation. However, our China doesn't even have the attitude of "you say you're right, she says she's right". Alas, what else can be said?

Spring at Longhua 323

-- Fei

Willows swaying, swallows nesting in pairs; this is the arrival of the charming spring. Peach blossoms smiling on the branches, weeping willows swaying by the river, all the scenery in nature shows a vibrant vitality.

"Spring outing to fragrant meadows, summer enjoyment of green lotus ponds;" this is indeed the joy of life! But we, for the sake of life, for the sake of the environment, have never had the opportunity to enjoy this blessing; let alone a blessing! Even the opportunity to take a trip to vent the coal gas in our chests is impossible. It's embarrassing to say. Since the beginning of spring this year, we have not seen a beautiful sun. It has always been gloomy, depressing weather, which is really annoying. Today, we finally saw a clear day; this is the first clear day this spring. How exciting it is! This day is rare, how can we let it pass lightly?

Li suggested going to New Shanghai, and An said: There's nothing fun in New Shanghai, it's better to go to Longhua. I'm easy, New Shanghai is fine, Longhua is fine too; but, after everyone discussed it, we decided to go to Longhua. The three of us, dragging our heavy steps, stepped onto the long Longhua Road; walking forward while talking and laughing, our hearts filled with many light feelings.

The broad beans and wheat in the fields, the rape flowers, green and yellow, resembled a beautiful natural painting. A fragrance of broad beans mixed with rape seed flowers, directly pounced into our nostrils, and invaded everyone's hearts and spleens. Birds chirping, frogs croaking, all broadcasting their happy songs and rhythmic sounds in nature. We were in it, as if we had entered another world, and almost forgot all the troubles and depression we brought from the city.

Spring light! Beautiful spring light, you intoxicate people; intoxicate them, let them be intoxicated in your embrace!

Nature, lovely nature! You are so enviable!

In front of Longhua Temple, a large crowd of men, women, old and young were crowding; surging like a tide, hugging like bees, continuously pouring into the temple. There were many country women, like country girls, holding incense candles and ingots in their hands, hawking to every tourist and pilgrim.

A series of cars were driving straight into the temple: parked in the open space in front of the hall. From each car, a pair of modern people came out; these were the ancestors of the bourgeoisie.

In the main hall, red candles were inserted all over the frames, and incense smoke rose into the blue clouds. Those devout men and women were all piously bowing to the Bodhisattva, begging for longevity and blessings. Several monks were busy receiving several decent pilgrims. "Madam", "Grandma", "Master", "Sir", the sounds were broadcast from that lotus-tongued mouth. Li looked at it and couldn't help saying: "Monks are also snobbish!"

"Of course, monks are much more snobbish than laypeople!" An added in agreement.

I didn't say anything, just nodded casually. Because, at this time, I was paying attention to another thing --- two young men were teasing three young female students. ---

In the garden to the east, in a corner of the garden, there was a pavilion, with a couple sitting inside telling love stories; face to face, shoulder to shoulder, talking with great relish. In the center of the garden was a teahouse, with a sign hanging that read, "Fragrant Tea, One Dime per Pot". There was also a snack shop, and all kinds of grocery stalls were also available. Back in front of the hall, several country children said to us: "Do you want to see the Great Buddha? We can lead you to see it." We just smiled and didn't answer them. There were many flower sellers standing at the door, selling magnolias, magnolias, canaries, and double-petal peaches, everything. Li wanted to buy a bunch of magnolias, and An wanted to buy a bunch of double-petal peaches; I said, "These flowers are going to wither, what do you want them for?" Later, they finally didn't buy them.

We stepped into the Repaying Kindness Pagoda, and a red paper strip that read, "Tourists Climbing the Pagoda, One Dime per Person" appeared before our eyes. We paid the price of three dimes and were able to climb the seven-story pagoda, looking far and wide, the lakes and mountains were like paintings, the desolate countryside, the scenery was in our arms. At this time, we were as happy as if we had ascended from hell to heaven.

On the way back, we wanted to take the train to the South Station, but unexpectedly, because we were too busy looking at the scenery outside the window, we passed the station; we staged a comical scene. When the ticket inspector came to check the tickets, and it became clear, everyone couldn't help laughing at the time, there was such a thing. The ticket inspector kindly told us to get off at Xinzhuang and take the 6 o'clock train back to Shanghai.

When we arrived at Xinzhuang, we all said that this was really unexpected, that we would come to visit Xinzhuang today. Although we waited in Xinzhuang for more than an hour, we almost explored all the towns here.

It is said that there will be a lantern festival here today! This is the "Lantern Festival celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's victory over the bandits." There are four dragons and ten lions, so beautiful. An wanted to watch the lantern festival before returning to Shanghai, but there was no night train, so she didn't succeed. In the end, she didn't have time to watch it.

After six o'clock, we were all still hungry, because there was no good food in the town; but finally, like two long snakes, the train brought the three empty shells of confusion, and left Xinzhuang and advanced towards the long journey.

Spring Rain on the Bund 324

-- Wen Hei

The spring rain on the Bund was falling in fine strands. On the Bund, I looked at the magnificent buildings of the factories in Pudong across the river, hidden in the mist. The coolies on the docks were carrying goods up and down the ships that brought the remaining products of their foreign countries to the Chinese market to dump. The sounds of "Hang yo, hang yo" and the whistles of the small steamships on the river were harmonizing. A wanderer wearing an old winter coat and carrying a cracked paper umbrella stood at the tram stop at the intersection of Nanjing Road, waiting for the tram. This person was neither a hero who bore heavy burdens and went far away, nor a little beggar who made a living by picking up crickets. He was an average person like the bustling masses. At this time, he came from the French Concession, waiting to take the tram to North Sichuan Road to borrow money from a friend. What did he borrow money for? Of course, like the ordinary and poor masses on the Shanghai Bund, he borrowed money to pay rent and food bills.

The spring rain was like an affectionate woman, drizzling and falling in a lingering manner, but the wanderer, who had things on his mind and no time to appreciate the rain scene on the Bund, felt annoyed and depressed. At ordinary times, he might feel that the drizzling rain scene, with streets and houses hidden in the mist, had a poetic picture, or it might arouse his creative impulse, or he might improvise a poem or two, or write one or two essays. However, at this time, the landlady's cold face and the restaurant owner's smilingly hypocritical expression were still lingering on his mind. He was also worried about whether the friend he was going to borrow money from was at home, and even if he was at home, whether he would have money to lend him. He didn't feel any creative impulse at all, and he had no interest in appreciating the scenery of the Bund under the spring rain.

The tram was always late in arriving. Our wanderer, holding a broken umbrella, stood in front of the Cathay Hotel and had no choice but to constantly run to the intersection of Nanjing Road and stretch his neck to look towards the ball park, but no matter how long he waited, it didn't come. Today, the No. 1 tram was deliberately making fun of him. He looked at the clock tower of the Jianghai Customs, it was already 4:50. He became more and more anxious. If his friend was not at home, and he was out for dinner, what should he do? He didn't have money for the return trip! He looked at the copper coins in the pocket of his old coat, which he had actually been playing with in his hand for a long time, which were only enough for one tram ride. He regretted buying a pack of cigarettes just now, thinking that he would definitely be able to borrow money. As soon as he thought of cigarettes, his subconscious mind taught him to take out a cigarette from his pocket, light it, and smoke it. It was supposed to dispel some depression and boredom. An old man from the countryside, also wearing an old coat, walked towards him in the rain, "Sir, I don't have money to go home..." and asked him for alms. This aroused a smile in his heart. He thought, "I can barely pity myself, and you're asking me to pity you!"

The spring rain on the Bund was drizzling and falling in a lingering manner, as if the sky was also weeping.

Viewing a Women's Young Men's Christian Association (YMCA) Women Workers' Play (Part 1) 325

— Ling He

On the afternoon of the 28th of last month, the Women's YMCA on Yuanmingyuan Road held a performance by women workers. Thanks to a friend's introduction, I had the opportunity to attend.

Having never seen a workers' play before, this experience provided me with many valuable lessons. Below, I would like to share some of my personal thoughts. Since the May Fourth Movement, China has seen the beginnings of modern drama. When I was in middle school, I was drawn to this new trend out of personal interest. We probably haven't forgotten that plays at that time lacked complete scripts, or even any scripts at all. It seemed that the world's famous plays were superfluous to China, and it was also true that the general public didn't understand them at all. This phenomenon persisted for a long time. The so-called "civilized plays" were simply a few clever performers improvising on stage, eliciting insincere laughter and tears. Until recently, we still saw so-called "spoken dramas" in various amusement parks, staging "Pearl Tower" type civilized plays, a clear case of false advertising. At the same time, in recent years, Chinese drama has progressed significantly in both content and form, thanks to the efforts of many progressive playwrights, certainly more so than when we were children. Therefore, the drama movement in China has a considerable foundation. This means that, due to the rapid progress of the audience, the essence of drama

Page 21

has been deeply understood by a segment of the population.

The question we should ask here is: Why does "civilized drama" still exist today? Of course, there is a social basis for this.

I remember five years ago, I had the opportunity to perform as a coal miner for an audience of shop employees. In the noisy crowd, our performance had almost zero impact, even though we performed sincerely and diligently. However, their impromptu performance of "Wang Xiao'er Celebrates the New Year" was very well-received. Also, not long ago, we performed half of "Noble People" during Children's Day. Because we didn't know beforehand that the audience was entirely elementary school students, they didn't understand "Noble People," and we made a big joke of ourselves. However, their children's play, "Sparrow and Child,"

made them very happy. Similarly, in amusement parks, in front of the "civilized drama" stage, there are always many audience members who enjoy the performance.

These are all valuable lessons: audiences with limited understanding cannot appreciate material that is beyond them, otherwise our performances will become laughable. Regarding this point, the women workers' play at the Women's YMCA

provides valuable insight. They performed three plays: "Little Red Padded Jacket," "Sister Xiang," and "Street Scene at Night."

"Little Red Padded Jacket" is a three-act play about a poor family. The mother makes a red padded jacket for someone else, but the little daughter thinks her mother is making it for her. The mother deceives the daughter, saying she is making it for her to wear during the New Year. When the New Year arrives, the little daughter sees the red padded jacket being worn by someone else

and starts crying. The choice of subject matter and the theme of this play are, of course, ordinary and realistic. However, there is no fixed script, and the so-called three acts each only last two or three minutes. But every actor is very casual, without the so-called serious atmosphere of the stage. However, both the dialogue and the actors' movements are very colloquial, and every audience member can understand them. In particular, they speak in the Shanghai dialect, and their movements are in the style of "civilized drama," which they are very familiar with. These are the main conditions that determine the success of the performance. On the other hand, in terms of the drama itself, the demands are very low, and it is very naive. Perhaps gentlemen and ladies will not be able to help but laugh. (To be continued)

Conflict 327

— Bai

Since the promotion of the New Life Movement, the student community can be considered the most vigorous in its implementation. Posting slogans, holding speech contests, everything is done with the air of "transforming into a perfect New Youth within five minutes." This week, our school also has a so-called "dormitory cleanliness competition." The student council has also appointed inspection committee members to conduct on-site inspections of each dormitory to show that they are serious about their work, and that they will do what they say. And there are also methods of warning and reward. 'Beneath heavy rewards, there must be brave men.'

However, unfortunately, a dispute ensued. Anyone passing by Dormitory Four could see a declaration posted high on the door, which was quite striking. It is recorded as follows:

Declaration of the Residents of Dormitory Four

We do not seek superficial cleanliness, but we guarantee the cleanliness of our character! Go to Dormitory Four and you will find a clean and simple

setting, but there are absolutely no books that corrupt the mind, nor are there expressions of despicable behavior. We disregard the superficial; we value the inner self!

Of course, you will not find the cleanliness you seek in our dormitory---although we have the cleanliness that you do not want---please go back!

Our slogan is: "We say what we can do, and we do what we say." Don't go crazy for some false honor! Do not be a tail-wagging sycophant? Do not blindly follow. Do not imitate hooligans.

"Men of fame are naturally carefree."

This declaration and slogan are obviously an attack. Perhaps the students think that the occurrence of this incident is unfortunate, and that it is dishonorable to publicize it to the outside world; but I think this is precisely the exposure that has long been needed, the exposure of the dark side of the student community. It is not just our school, similar disputes are constantly brewing and breaking out in schools in various provinces and regions. Not talking about the dispute itself, the background of this dispute is worth mentioning. I don't need to say things like "Every student is a member of the student council, and should do their best for the student council and promote its perfection," because everyone knows that. But, or perhaps everyone also knows that the student council is just like a corner of society, with struggles, suspicions, connections, and sabotage, with... all the dark sides of society first sprouting in schools. How to struggle, how to connect, those who have been through school understand, and there is no need to waste words. It is in this way that this dispute has been brewing for quite some time before erupting.

I have a general feeling of anger towards the residents of Dormitory Four---I am dissatisfied with the organization of the student council, but I do not sympathize with their actions. Those who do not understand the truth think that they are bad elements, troublemakers, deliberately sabotaging the New Life Movement, and will never forgive them for feeling dissatisfied with the imperfection of the student council. Our Chinese teacher once said, "The New Life Movement is difficult to implement among three types of people, one of whom is men of fame." They insist on shouting the slogan "Men of fame are naturally carefree," wouldn't that make it even more certain? But, indeed, the student council often becomes a small political stage; with struggles, suspicions, sabotage, and connections, just like those highly self-regarded hermits venting their grievances against despicable politicians, this dispute erupted for this reason.

School? 328

— Qing

It is already the fourth year, and they are still admitting such a large group of new students. This has been questioning in my heart for a long time, and the answer I got is: the school is only seeking tuition revenue, and the students are just muddling through to buy a diploma.

Six new classmates came to our class, and somehow they all became close friends in a short time. I learned from hearsay that the origins of these people are unclear, and what I saw with my own eyes is enough to prove that the rumors are true. The gold-trimmed Western suits are bought, but I haven't seen them turn a page, or even come to class! Even if they come, they just ask someone to take attendance for them! Yes, the school is a hotel, the students' goal is to muddle through to get a diploma, and in the future China will produce several more high-level idlers.

Roughly speaking, there are a few of the six who have some special skills in books. Therefore, before any test or assignment, I always hear some of them say to one: "X! You read the book for tomorrow's test! We are busy playing, and we can't understand it anyway, so you have to take full responsibility! Roughly speaking, the professors are very careless, and once they become strict, if they don't allow a Pass, then please write a few more papers for us and hand them all in for us." Or "XX course papers are needed tomorrow, X, you just do a few more pages. Actually, when you hand it in to the teacher, will he really correct it for you? Reading is really meaningless, so I haven't even bothered to buy books recently, if I have money to buy books, I won't buy things to eat; ha---ha---it's really funny, besides us, there are many people in our class who are working as scribes, and all the homework is copied from others..." Three months have passed like this, and the monthly exams are considered Passed, haha, what have they gained? The monthly exams can pass like this, what about the final exams? Let's see what they do!

One afternoon, I discovered that the six of them were whispering in the campus, I walked past them, and accidentally heard; "Don't worry about the final exams, I have already planned it for you. I guarantee you will graduate with a square cap." Ah! Their magic power is really great, no wonder they can be so happy. But the money of fathers and brothers is only used as a tool to buy diplomas. But what exactly is a diploma such a big deal? Can it definitely solve our lives?

Roughly speaking, their finances have run out! Otherwise, why don't they eat lavishly like before? Why are they borrowing money from people? Therefore, I also heard that one of the six is planning to seduce the daughter of a wealthy businessman in XXX middle school, and it is said that he has already spent a lot of her money.

I came to this highest institution of learning from my hometown with enthusiasm, but what I have seen and heard everywhere is disheartening. Ah! The university is just this kind of "school", and university life is just like this!

Miss Katsuko 329

— Bai Rong

The thin twilight of late autumn.

A quiet street: the sound of people, the sound of cars and horses have long disappeared in the air, what cannot be eliminated is the catkin-like clouds滞 lingering above the head. Piles and piles decorate the sky, like ancient brocade. The setting sun, like a lazy tourist, gazes at its future vaguely and melancholically. From the horizon, from the treetops, dusk so easily flows in, it pours into this cool street, blue paving stones, round windows full of poetry, a garden decorated with vines in August, and then gradually disappears in the dim lights, and the night comes to cover everything in front of us.

It's quiet, quiet and a little cold, wutong leaves floating everywhere like the thoughts of someone who has left their home.

Even the street lights are cold.

Perpendicular to the shadow of the street lamp, black, is a young girl's body, a slender figure, leaning on the side, with the desolate taste of a late-blooming flower, in the evening wind, everything is floating: skirt, hair, plain body······ the only thing that does not move is that fixed gaze containing sorrow.

This gaze is staring ahead.

In front, there are deep lights, deep shadows of trees, deep night, all black. But in front of her life, like this, is also unfolding such a black picture, and it is a panoramic black, rough, blurry, dim, without street lights radiating light, without tree shadows that add beauty, and that pavement, there is only a dark night scene, no motherland, no home, no relatives, she is lonely being abandoned in this trampling big city, she has to pretend to smile and comfort strangers every day, wearing away her youth like this, but she is not a bad person, she needs love, can love, knows how to love, but people just don't want these things, thinking of this, she reluctantly looked at the sycamore leaves飘 fluttering on the ground.

One piece, two pieces, three pieces, so circling, dancing····· two pieces, three pieces, four pieces, circling, dancing, so rushing forward····· rushing to the gauze window透 passing the sound of the piano--

It is not clear whether it is orange or madder, a piece of gauze so tight that it flattens from the treetops of the扁 pine, like the beautiful moon of the remnant night, singing flows out from there, as light as a forgotten childhood dream. Swinging to the street, swinging to the corner of the fence, and then disappearing in the darkness, hearing such a gentle tune, who wouldn't think of their own home?

Yes, she couldn't help but quietly think of her own home.

But "home," such a kind and familiar word, in her memory can only evoke some unpleasant impressions. It is not that she has no home, her home is in the distant, distant east of the sea, a land of ancient customs, filled with brilliant cherry blossoms. She remembers that when she was ten years old, because her parents could not afford it, she carried such a light small bag, containing childish and ridiculous tears, and was brought to this ancient China by her uncle. When she first came, she was not used to anything, but now, can't she use a foreign language to maintain her own survival? Isn't she穿 coming and going every day on the streets and alleys, as if in her own homeland? Thinking of this, some dreamy feelings came to her heart. Eight years have passed, but these eight years have not passed quietly! Eight years ago, no one would have thought that they would fall into this kind of state, in fact, as long as her uncle was alive, she would not have this day of East floating and West lodging.

The dissatisfaction of real life provokes memories that have not been revisited for a long time, and she thinks of her uncle again----

Thin and tall, with a smile on his face, he often put himself in a square kimono, peacefully smoking cheap paper cigarettes, calculating the accounts under the lamp, so smoking and calculating, eight years slipped past from his hands. But in the spring of that year, I don't know what kind of demon he was caught up in, he even ran to Hongkou regardless of the property in the store, to do some便便衣隊去 plainclothes team work. The machine gun rang all night, and the threat of death pushed her to this quiet concession. Following that was the cannon, right? Following that was blood, right? Following that was the shout of killing that lit up the sky with fire, right? No one collected the remains, they were piled up, of course they are easily forgotten, like her uncle, her friends, like many Chinese people.

Therefore, on the other hand, when people wanted champagne, she ended up working as a waitress in this hotel.

Her name is Katsuko, for the sake of sounding better, it is now changed to Meilian.

She has a beautiful face, a little silence, and a little pure heart.

She can smile lightly, but now, she can't laugh.

Placed in front of her, behind her, left and right, the past life is like a magical web, so entangled, rotating, that the scenery really makes people 目迷 dizzying·······

"The authority of the Empire! Homeless travelers!"

Sighing, she pulled her clothes, locked her worries in her heart, and dragged her lazy steps forward, passing through a dark street like this.

It's quiet, quiet and a little cold, wutong leaves floating like the thoughts of someone who has left their home.

Unexpected Harvest 330

— Xiao Ying

"Yes, this, this, is the harvest I had imagined!" Ming, pondering, couldn't stop the excitement from washing over his mind.

The time was the season of mid-spring. Humph, "spring", what a charming word! That "spring love" spread over the hearts of young people, that "spring wind" kissed everyone's faces; gently, softly, sweetly, blowing, floating. The peach blossoms in the vase were welcoming it with smiling faces, the rosy cheeks of the girls revealed intoxicating dimples, the Western women half-naked showed their seductive bodies, that······ these, active, turbulent, mixed with a charming charm, but completely ineffective for Ming.

Under the 75W milky white light bulb, it emitted a bright light, swallowing all parts of the room. Right there on the nearby table, a piece of paper whiter than the light was lying quietly, on which, the strong and powerful handwriting created by the Waterman ink and the Parker gold nib was swaying and pacing into Ming's eyes.

I don't know if it was emotion or stimulation? He just silently leaned on the edge of the table. His eyes blurred, as if a layer of light silk covered his eyeballs, and he stared blankly in a daze.

When a gust of autumn wind in spring blew past, how cool it was! Then, he woke up. Involuntarily, recalling and thinking!

That was in mid-autumn a few months ago, I don't know if my friends were intentionally joking or sincerely saying;

--Ming, why don't you write a novel? No, a novella is fine, it's more satisfying than a short story.

--Hum, write? Satisfying? Write what? What is satisfying? Come on, don't fantasize! The result of fantasizing will be encounters that shatter your imagination. At the time, Ming had also secretly thought this.

Immediately, he realized something, because he knew himself, how could a moron like himself be praised by friends? Undoubtedly, they were mocking themselves, that is, an insult to themselves!

Humans ultimately have a heart of "upwardness," no, it's more real to say "anger" than to say upwardness. Because of this, his mood was disturbed for many days.

---However, what genre to use?······ Bankrupt

rural area? Yes, how fashionable, taking this kind of subject matter is as fresh as "taking advantage of the fire to rob." But, no, I have never squatted in the countryside, and I don't know whether the sun is red or white when it comes out. This, is the first shot in my life, and it must be as powerful as a blooming bomb, and it must never be so reckless.····· Then, fleeing famine? Famine year? War disaster? Yes, it also has the same effect as before, but·······

---Finally, he discovered this sentence: "Literature is the precursor of all social trends, and a reflection of life." Really, according to this principle, I should write what is reflected in my life, that is not only powerful, but also can arouse sympathy, maybe····· hey!

The manuscript was finally completed under the condition of "nothing is difficult in the world, just afraid of thick skin." Then, what made him

The difficulty that arose was: "Where to submit it", in this modern society with different doors? At this point, distress tightened around him, and the courage from before diminished.

After all, the manuscript was sent out, and the place it was accepted was a publication that flaunted "no prejudice, welcome external manuscripts." Gently, Ming sighed three times, and all the weight seemed to be removed.

A week, two weeks,······ published, did not see his name on the advertisement, and published again, the same vague; a spoonful of cold water extinguished the flame in his heart, he thought: "Isn't it published? No, no, then, why don't you send it back? Humph, who knows!" Suspicion, destruction, frustration, all kinds of emotions were fighting with each other　　One evening when the lights were on, the postman delivered a large envelope, vaguely, the handwriting on the envelope was jumping along with his heart. Opened it, is it? Original manuscript, untouched, is considered polite? Also attached such a clean piece of letter paper; this, is somewhat of a loss.

·····Your manuscript has been read, the beauty of the wording and the depth of the meaning are very admirable,····· but because····· temporarily······ so······ Still pray······ is the prayer·····

Some people say that the mystery of Chinese characters lies in the application of "beginning, continuation, transition, and combination." Here, it is clear that the meaning is "the text is simple and cannot be applied", but under the "transition and combination" situation, the traces are completely erased. The unstoppable excitement was washing over Ming's mind, he pondered----

----Yes, this, I had imagined it long ago. Humph, no prejudice? External manuscripts? Scam, in short, this is the only harvest of an unknown literary beggar!

Tomorrow (9) 331

— Mu Lin

Although I hope the days will pass quickly, this is the last day, and I should cherish the last day of my flower-like life.
